     1→# Brainwave: Real-Time Speech Recognition and Summarization Tool
     2→
     3→## Table of Contents
     4→
     5→1. [Introduction](#introduction)
     6→2. [Deployment](#deployment)
     7→3. [Code Structure & Architecture](#code-structure--architecture)
     8→4. [Testing](#testing)
     9→
    10→---
    11→
    12→## Introduction
    13→
    14→### Background
    15→
    16→In the era of rapid information exchange, capturing and organizing ideas swiftly is paramount. **Brainwave** addresses this need by providing a robust speech recognition input method that allows users to effortlessly input their thoughts, regardless of their initial organization. Leveraging advanced technologies, Brainwave transforms potentially messy and unstructured verbal inputs into coherent and logical summaries, enhancing productivity and idea management.
    17→
    18→### Goals
    19→
    20→- **Efficient Speech Recognition:** Enable users to quickly input ideas through speech, reducing the friction of manual typing.
    21→- **Organized Summarization:** Automatically process and summarize spoken input into structured and logical formats.
    22→- **Multilingual Support:** Cater to a diverse user base by supporting multiple languages, ensuring accessibility and convenience.
    23→
    24→### Technical Advantages
    25→
    26→1. **Real-Time Processing:**
    27→   - **Low Latency:** Processes audio streams in real-time, providing immediate transcription and summarization, which is essential for maintaining the flow of thoughts.
    28→   - **Continuous Interaction:** Unlike traditional batch processing systems, Brainwave offers seamless real-time interaction, ensuring that users receive timely response on their inputs.
    29→
    30→2. **Multilingual Proficiency:**
    31→   - **Diverse Language Support:** Handles inputs in multiple languages without the need for separate processing pipelines, enhancing versatility and user accessibility.
    32→   - **Automatic Language Detection:** Identifies the language of the input automatically, streamlining the user experience.
    33→
    34→3. **Sophisticated Text Processing:**
    35→   - **Error Correction:** Utilizes advanced algorithms to identify and correct errors inherent in speech recognition, ensuring accurate transcriptions.
    36→   - **Readability Enhancement:** Improves punctuation and structure of the transcribed text, making summaries clear and professional.
    37→   - **Intent Recognition:** Understands the context and intent behind the spoken words, enabling the generation of meaningful summaries.
    38→
    39→---
    40→
    41→## Deployment
    42→
    43→Deploying **Brainwave** involves setting up a Python-based environment, installing the necessary dependencies, and launching the server to handle real-time speech recognition and summarization. Follow the steps below to get started:
    44→
    45→### Prerequisites
    46→
    47→- **Python 3.8+**: Ensure that Python is installed on your system. You can download it from the [official website](https://www.python.org/downloads/).
    48→- **Virtual Environment Tool**: It's recommended to use `venv` or `virtualenv` to manage project dependencies.
    49→
    50→### Setup Steps
    51→
    52→1. **Clone the Repository**
    53→
    54→   ```bash
    55→   git clone https://github.com/grapeot/brainwave.git
    56→   cd brainwave
    57→   ```
    58→
    59→2. **Create a Virtual Environment**
    60→
    61→   ```bash
    62→   python3 -m venv venv
    63→   ```
    64→
    65→3. **Activate the Virtual Environment**
    66→
    67→   - **On macOS/Linux:**
    68→
    69→     ```bash
    70→     source venv/bin/activate
    71→     ```
    72→
    73→   - **On Windows:**
    74→
    75→     ```bash
    76→     venv\Scripts\activate
    77→     ```
    78→
    79→4. **Install Dependencies**
    80→
    81→   Ensure that you have `pip` updated, then install the required packages:
    82→
    83→   ```bash
    84→   pip install --upgrade pip
    85→   pip install -r requirements.txt
    86→   ```
    87→
    88→5. **Configure Environment Variables**
    89→
    90→   Brainwave requires the OpenAI API key to function. You can set it via environment variables or a `.env` file (loaded via `python-dotenv`):
    91→
    92→   - **Required:** `OPENAI_API_KEY` – for realtime transcription and Readability/Correctness
    93→   - **Optional:** `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL` – default `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15`; `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODALITIES` – default `text`
    94→   - **For Readability/Correctness (Gemini):** `GOOGLE_API_KEY` – for Gemini-based text enhancement
    95→
    96→   - **On macOS/Linux:**
    97→
    98→     ```bash
    99→     export OPENAI_API_KEY='your-openai-api-key'
   100→     ```
   101→
   102→   - **On Windows (Command Prompt):**
   103→
   104→     ```cmd
   105→     set OPENAI_API_KEY=your-openai-api-key
   106→     ```
   107→
   108→   - **On Windows (PowerShell):**
   109→
   110→     ```powershell
   111→     $env:OPENAI_API_KEY="your-openai-api-key"
   112→     ```
   113→
   114→6. **Launch the Server**
   115→
   116→   Start the FastAPI server using Uvicorn:
   117→
   118→   ```bash
   119→   uvicorn realtime_server:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 3005
   120→   ```
   121→
   122→   The server will be accessible at `http://localhost:3005`.
   123→
   124→7. **Access the Application**
   125→
   126→   Open your web browser and navigate to `http://localhost:3005` to interact with Brainwave's speech recognition interface.
   127→
   128→---
   129→
   130→## Code Structure & Architecture
   131→
   132→Understanding the architecture of **Brainwave** provides insights into its real-time processing capabilities and multilingual support. The project is organized into several key components, each responsible for distinct functionalities.
   133→
   134→### 1. **Backend**
   135→
   136→#### a. `realtime_server.py`
   137→
   138→- **Framework:** Utilizes **FastAPI** to handle HTTP and WebSocket connections, offering high performance and scalability.
   139→- **WebSocket Endpoint:** Establishes a `/api/v1/ws` endpoint for real-time audio streaming between the client and server.
   140→- **Audio Processing:**
   141→  - **`AudioProcessor` Class:** Resamples incoming audio data from 48kHz to 24kHz to match OpenAI's requirements.
   142→  - **Buffer Management:** Accumulates audio chunks for efficient processing and transmission.
   143→- **Concurrency:** Employs `asyncio` to manage asynchronous tasks for receiving and sending audio data, ensuring non-blocking operations.
   144→- **Logging:** Implements comprehensive logging to monitor connections, data flow, and potential errors.
   145→
   146→#### b. `openai_realtime_client.py`
   147→
   148→- **WebSocket Client:** Manages the connection to OpenAI's real-time API, facilitating the transmission of audio data and reception of transcriptions.
   149→- **Session Management:** Handles session creation, updates, and closure, ensuring a stable and persistent connection.
   150→- **Event Handlers:** Registers and manages handlers for various message types from OpenAI, allowing for customizable responses and actions based on incoming data.
   151→- **Error Handling:** Incorporates robust mechanisms to handle and log connection issues or unexpected messages.
   152→
   153→#### c. `prompts.py`
   154→
   155→- **Prompt Definitions:** Contains a dictionary of prompts in both Chinese and English, tailored for tasks such as paraphrasing, readability enhancement, and generating insightful summaries.
   156→- **Customization:** Allows for easy modification and extension of prompts to cater to different processing requirements or languages.
   157→
   158→### 2. **Frontend**
   159→
   160→#### a. `static/realtime.html`
   161→
   162→- **User Interface:** Provides a clean and responsive UI for users to interact with Brainwave, featuring:
   163→  - **Model Selection:** Dropdown to choose between `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15` (default) and `gpt-realtime-1.5`.
   164→  - **Recording Controls:** A toggle button to start and stop audio recording.
   165→  - **Transcript Display:** A section to display the transcribed and summarized text in real-time.
   166→  - **Copy Functionality:** Enables users to easily copy the summarized text.
   167→  - **Timer:** Visual feedback to indicate recording duration.
   168→
   169→- **Styling:** Utilizes CSS to ensure a modern and user-friendly appearance, optimized for both desktop and mobile devices.
   170→
   171→- **Audio Handling:**
   172→  - **Web Audio API:** Captures audio streams from the user's microphone, processes them into the required format, and handles chunking for transmission.
   173→  - **WebSocket Integration:** Establishes and manages the WebSocket connection to the backend server, ensuring seamless data flow.
   174→
   175→### 3. **Configuration**
   176→
   177→#### a. `config.py`
   178→
   179→- **Model & Modalities:** Loads `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL` (default `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15`) and `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODALITIES` (default `text`) from environment variables.
   180→
   181→#### b. `requirements.txt`
   182→
   183→Lists all Python dependencies required to run Brainwave, ensuring that the environment is set up with compatible packages:
   184→
   185→### 4. **Prompts & Text Processing**
   186→
   187→Brainwave leverages a suite of predefined prompts to enhance text processing capabilities:
   188→
   189→- **Paraphrasing:** Corrects speech-to-text errors and improves punctuation without altering the original meaning (used for realtime transcription).
   190→- **Readability Enhancement:** Improves the readability of transcribed text by adding appropriate punctuation and formatting.
   191→- **Correctness Check:** Analyzes text for factual accuracy.
   192→
   193→These prompts are meticulously crafted to ensure that the transcribed text is not only accurate but also contextually rich and user-friendly.
   194→
   195→### 5. **Logging & Monitoring**
   196→
   197→Comprehensive logging is integrated throughout the backend components to monitor:
   198→
   199→- **Connection Status:** Tracks WebSocket connections and disconnections.
   200→- **Data Transmission:** Logs the size and status of audio chunks being processed and sent.
   201→- **Error Reporting:** Captures and logs any errors or exceptions, facilitating easier debugging and maintenance.
   202→
   203→### 6. **Local Storage Replay Feature (IndexedDB)**
   204→
   205→Brainwave includes a browser-based replay feature that allows users to replay their most recent recording session if recognition fails, network is interrupted, or backend errors occur.
   206→
   207→#### Overview
   208→
   209→- **Purpose:** Persist audio chunks and control events (start/stop) to browser local storage during recording, enabling replay without re-speaking.
   210→- **Storage:** Uses IndexedDB (not localStorage) for binary data support and larger capacity (typically GB-level).
   211→- **Scope:** Only keeps the most recent session by default to avoid unlimited storage usage. If local storage is unavailable, real-time recording still works (but replay is disabled).
   212→
   213→#### Technical Details
   214→
   215→**Storage Model:**
   216→- **Database:** `brainwave-replay`, version `1`
   217→- **Object Stores:**
   218→  - `sessions` (keyPath: `id`, autoIncrement: true)
   219→    - Fields: `id`, `createdAt`, `status` ("recording"|"completed"|"failed"), `sampleRate` (default 24000), `channelCount` (1), `durationMs`, `error`
   220→  - `chunks` (keyPath: `id`, autoIncrement: true, index `sessionId`)
   221→    - Fields: `sessionId`, `seq`, `deltaMs` (time offset from start for replay throttling), `kind` ("start"|"audio"|"stop"|"meta"), `payload` (Blob or ArrayBuffer), `byteLength`
   222→
   223→**Storage Size Estimation:**
   224→- 24000 sample rate, 16-bit mono => 48KB/second
   225→- Only keeps the most recent N sessions (e.g., 5 sessions or total < 100MB)
   226→- Oldest sessions and their chunks are deleted when quota is exceeded
   227→
   228→**Recording Workflow:**
   229→1. On `startRecording` success: Create session, write a `kind: "start"` record with `deltaMs = 0`
   230→2. During `onaudioprocess`: When sending each 24k-sample chunk to backend, also call `appendChunk(sessionId, { seq, deltaMs, kind: "audio", payload: sendBuffer })`. `deltaMs` is calculated using `performance.now()` relative to session start to maintain original timing.
   231→3. On `stopRecording`: After sending the last chunk, write a `kind: "stop"` record, update `sessions.status = "completed"`, and record `durationMs`
   232→4. Cleanup: After recording ends, trigger `enforceQuota({ maxSessions: 5, maxBytes: 100 * 1024 * 1024 })`
   233→5. Fallback: If IndexedDB initialization fails (no permission, incognito mode quota restrictions, etc.), set an in-memory fallback flag, only send in real-time without prompts, and disable the replay button
   234→
   235→**Replay Workflow:**
   236→1. **Session Selection:** Default to replaying the most recent `status = "completed"` session
   237→2. **State Check:** If currently recording/generating, prompt user to stop before replaying
   238→3. **Connection:** Create a new WebSocket connection (or reuse existing, ensuring backend accepts new start/stop sequences; prefer new connection)
   239→4. **Replay Steps:**
   240→   - Send `kind: "start"` control message (consistent with current protocol, e.g., `{type: "start_recording"}`)
   241→   - Send audio chunks in recorded order
   242→   - Audio chunk sending uses `setTimeout` based on `deltaMs` timing; if timing is too dense, set minimum interval of 5-10ms to prevent blocking
   243→   - Send `kind: "stop"` control message at the end
   244→5. **Error Handling:** On errors (WebSocket closed, backend 4xx/5xx, etc.), log and prompt but keep session data for retry
   245→
   246→**Backend Compatibility:**
   247→- WebSocket protocol remains consistent: `start_recording` control message -> binary PCM chunks -> `stop_recording`. Replay follows the same protocol.
   248→- Backend allows multiple new connections from the same browser in a short time; if not allowed, frontend should wait for existing connection to return to idle before replaying
   249→
   250→**UI/UX:**
   251→- Add a "Replay Last Recording" button near the record button, with states: available/disabled/replaying
   252→- Disable record button during replay, show progress (based on `deltaMs` and chunk count)
   253→- If local storage is unavailable or quota insufficient, show reason in button tooltip
   254→
   255→---
   256→
   257→## Testing
   258→
   259→Brainwave includes a comprehensive test suite to ensure reliability and maintainability. The tests cover various components:
   260→
   261→- **Audio Processing Tests:** Verify the correct handling of audio data, including resampling and buffer management.
   262→- **LLM Integration Tests:** Test the integration with language models (GPT and Gemini) for text processing.
   263→- **API Endpoint Tests:** Ensure the FastAPI endpoints work correctly, including streaming responses.
   264→- **WebSocket Tests:** Verify real-time communication for audio streaming.
   265→
   266→To run the tests:
   267→
   268→1. **Install Test Dependencies**
   269→
   270→   The test dependencies are included in `requirements.txt` (pytest, pytest-cov, pytest-asyncio, pytest-mock, httpx). Make sure they are installed:
   271→   ```bash
   272→   pip install -r requirements.txt
   273→   ```
   274→
   275→2. **Run Tests**
   276→
   277→   ```bash
   278→   # Run all tests
   279→   pytest tests/
   280→
   281→   # Run tests with verbose output
   282→   pytest -v tests/
   283→
   284→   # Run tests for a specific component
   285→   pytest tests/test_audio_processor.py
   286→   ```
   287→
   288→3. **Test Environment**
   289→
   290→   Tests use mocked API clients to avoid actual API calls. Set up the test environment variables:
   291→   ```bash
   292→   export OPENAI_API_KEY='test_key'  # For local testing
   293→   export GOOGLE_API_KEY='test_key'  # For local testing
   294→   ```
   295→
   296→The test suite is designed to run without making actual API calls, making it suitable for CI/CD pipelines.
   297→

The project is organized into several key components, each responsible for distinct functionalities.\n   133\u2192\n   134\u2192### 1. **Backend**\n   135\u2192\n   136\u2192#### a. `realtime_server.py`\n   137\u2192\n   138\u2192- **Framework:** Utilizes **FastAPI** to handle HTTP and WebSocket connections, offering high performance and scalability.\n   139\u2192- **WebSocket Endpoint:** Establishes a `/api/v1/ws` endpoint for real-time audio streaming between the client and server.\n   140\u2192- **Audio Processing:**\n   141\u2192  - **`AudioProcessor` Class:** Resamples incoming audio data from 48kHz to 24kHz to match OpenAI's requirements.\n   142\u2192  - **Buffer Management:** Accumulates audio chunks for efficient processing and transmission.\n   143\u2192- **Concurrency:** Employs `asyncio` to manage asynchronous tasks for receiving and sending audio data, ensuring non-blocking operations.\n   144\u2192- **Logging:** Implements comprehensive logging to monitor connections, data flow, and potential errors.\n   145\u2192\n   146\u2192#### b. `openai_realtime_client.py`\n   147\u2192\n   148\u2192- **WebSocket Client:** Manages the connection to OpenAI's real-time API, facilitating the transmission of audio data and reception of transcriptions.\n   149\u2192- **Session Management:** Handles session creation, updates, and closure, ensuring a stable and persistent connection.\n   150\u2192- **Event Handlers:** Registers and manages handlers for various message types from OpenAI, allowing for customizable responses and actions based on incoming data.\n   151\u2192- **Error Handling:** Incorporates robust mechanisms to handle and log connection issues or unexpected messages.\n   152\u2192\n   153\u2192#### c. `prompts.py`\n   154\u2192\n   155\u2192- **Prompt Definitions:** Contains a dictionary of prompts in both Chinese and English, tailored for tasks such as paraphrasing, readability enhancement, and generating insightful summaries.\n   156\u2192- **Customization:** Allows for easy modification and extension of prompts to cater to different processing requirements or languages.\n   157\u2192\n   158\u2192### 2. **Frontend**\n   159\u2192\n   160\u2192#### a. `static/realtime.html`\n   161\u2192\n   162\u2192- **User Interface:** Provides a clean and responsive UI for users to interact with Brainwave, featuring:\n   163\u2192  - **Model Selection:** Dropdown to choose between `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15` (default) and `gpt-realtime-1.5`.\n   164\u2192  - **Recording Controls:** A toggle button to start and stop audio recording.\n   165\u2192  - **Transcript Display:** A section to display the transcribed and summarized text in real-time.\n   166\u2192  - **Copy Functionality:** Enables users to easily copy the summarized text.\n   167\u2192  - **Timer:** Visual feedback to indicate recording duration.\n   168\u2192\n   169\u2192- **Styling:** Utilizes CSS to ensure a modern and user-friendly appearance, optimized for both desktop and mobile devices.\n   170\u2192\n   171\u2192- **Audio Handling:**\n   172\u2192  - **Web Audio API:** Captures audio streams from the user's microphone, processes them into the required format, and handles chunking for transmission.\n   173\u2192  - **WebSocket Integration:** Establishes and manages the WebSocket connection to the backend server, ensuring seamless data flow.\n   174\u2192\n   175\u2192### 3. **Configuration**\n   176\u2192\n   177\u2192#### a. `config.py`\n   178\u2192\n   179\u2192- **Model & Modalities:** Loads `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL` (default `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15`) and `OPENAI_REALTIME_MODALITIES` (default `text`) from environment variables.\n   180\u2192\n   181\u2192#### b. `requirements.txt`\n   182\u2192\n   183\u2192Lists all Python dependencies required to run Brainwave, ensuring that the environment is set up with compatible packages:\n   184\u2192\n   185\u2192### 4. **Prompts & Text Processing**\n   186\u2192\n   187\u2192Brainwave leverages a suite of predefined prompts to enhance text processing capabilities:\n   188\u2192\n   189\u2192- **Paraphrasing:** Corrects speech-to-text errors and improves punctuation without altering the original meaning (used for realtime transcription).\n   190\u2192- **Readability Enhancement:** Improves the readability of transcribed text by adding appropriate punctuation and formatting.\n   191\u2192- **Correctness Check:** Analyzes text for factual accuracy.\n   192\u2192\n   193\u2192These prompts are meticulously crafted to ensure that the transcribed text is not only accurate but also contextually rich and user-friendly.\n   194\u2192\n   195\u2192### 5. **Logging & Monitoring**\n   196\u2192\n   197\u2192Comprehensive logging is integrated throughout the backend components to monitor:\n   198\u2192\n   199\u2192- **Connection Status:** Tracks WebSocket connections and disconnections.\n   200\u2192- **Data Transmission:** Logs the size and status of audio chunks being processed and sent.\n   201\u2192- **Error Reporting:** Captures and logs any errors or exceptions, facilitating easier debugging and maintenance.\n   202\u2192\n   203\u2192### 6. **Local Storage Replay Feature (IndexedDB)**\n   204\u2192\n   205\u2192Brainwave includes a browser-based replay feature that allows users to replay their most recent recording session if recognition fails, network is interrupted, or backend errors occur.\n   206\u2192\n   207\u2192#### Overview\n   208\u2192\n   209\u2192- **Purpose:** Persist audio chunks and control events (start/stop) to browser local storage during recording, enabling replay without re-speaking.\n   210\u2192- **Storage:** Uses IndexedDB (not localStorage) for binary data support and larger capacity (typically GB-level).\n   211\u2192- **Scope:** Only keeps the most recent session by default to avoid unlimited storage usage. If local storage is unavailable, real-time recording still works (but replay is disabled).\n   212\u2192\n   213\u2192#### Technical Details\n   214\u2192\n   215\u2192**Storage Model:**\n   216\u2192- **Database:** `brainwave-replay`, version `1`\n   217\u2192- **Object Stores:**\n   218\u2192  - `sessions` (keyPath: `id`, autoIncrement: true)\n   219\u2192    - Fields: `id`, `createdAt`, `status` (\"recording\"|\"completed\"|\"failed\"), `sampleRate` (default 24000), `channelCount` (1), `durationMs`, `error`\n   220\u2192  - `chunks` (keyPath: `id`, autoIncrement: true, index `sessionId`)\n   221\u2192    - Fields: `sessionId`, `seq`, `deltaMs` (time offset from start for replay throttling), `kind` (\"start\"|\"audio\"|\"stop\"|\"meta\"), `payload` (Blob or ArrayBuffer), `byteLength`\n   222\u2192\n   223\u2192**Storage Size Estimation:**\n   224\u2192- 24000 sample rate, 16-bit mono => 48KB/second\n   225\u2192- Only keeps the most recent N sessions (e.g., 5 sessions or total < 100MB)\n   226\u2192- Oldest sessions and their chunks are deleted when quota is exceeded\n   227\u2192\n   228\u2192**Recording Workflow:**\n   229\u21921. On `startRecording` success: Create session, write a `kind: \"start\"` record with `deltaMs = 0`\n   230\u21922. During `onaudioprocess`: When sending each 24k-sample chunk to backend, also call `appendChunk(sessionId, { seq, deltaMs, kind: \"audio\", payload: sendBuffer })`. `deltaMs` is calculated using `performance.now()` relative to session start to maintain original timing.\n   231\u21923. On `stopRecording`: After sending the last chunk, write a `kind: \"stop\"` record, update `sessions.status = \"completed\"`, and record `durationMs`\n   232\u21924. Cleanup: After recording ends, trigger `enforceQuota({ maxSessions: 5, maxBytes: 100 * 1024 * 1024 })`\n   233\u21925. Fallback: If IndexedDB initialization fails (no permission, incognito mode quota restrictions, etc.), set an in-memory fallback flag, only send in real-time without prompts, and disable the replay button\n   234\u2192\n   235\u2192**Replay Workflow:**\n   236\u21921. **Session Selection:** Default to replaying the most recent `status = \"completed\"` session\n   237\u21922. **State Check:** If currently recording/generating, prompt user to stop before replaying\n   238\u21923. **Connection:** Create a new WebSocket connection (or reuse existing, ensuring backend accepts new start/stop sequences; prefer new connection)\n   239\u21924. **Replay Steps:**\n   240\u2192   - Send `kind: \"start\"` control message (consistent with current protocol, e.g., `{type: \"start_recording\"}`)\n   241\u2192   - Send audio chunks in recorded order\n   242\u2192   - Audio chunk sending uses `setTimeout` based on `deltaMs` timing; if timing is too dense, set minimum interval of 5-10ms to prevent blocking\n   243\u2192   - Send `kind: \"stop\"` control message at the end\n   244\u21925. **Error Handling:** On errors (WebSocket closed, backend 4xx/5xx, etc.), log and prompt but keep session data for retry\n   245\u2192\n   246\u2192**Backend Compatibility:**\n   247\u2192- WebSocket protocol remains consistent: `start_recording` control message -> binary PCM chunks -> `stop_recording`. Replay follows the same protocol.\n   248\u2192- Backend allows multiple new connections from the same browser in a short time; if not allowed, frontend should wait for existing connection to return to idle before replaying\n   249\u2192\n   250\u2192**UI/UX:**\n   251\u2192- Add a \"Replay Last Recording\" button near the record button, with states: available/disabled/replaying\n   252\u2192- Disable record button during replay, show progress (based on `deltaMs` and chunk count)\n   253\u2192- If local storage is unavailable or quota insufficient, show reason in button tooltip\n   254\u2192\n   255\u2192---\n   256\u2192\n   257\u2192## Testing\n   258\u2192\n   259\u2192Brainwave includes a comprehensive test suite to ensure reliability and maintainability. The tests cover various components:\n   260\u2192\n   261\u2192- **Audio Processing Tests:** Verify the correct handling of audio data, including resampling and buffer management.\n   262\u2192- **LLM Integration Tests:** Test the integration with language models (GPT and Gemini) for text processing.\n   263\u2192- **API Endpoint Tests:** Ensure the FastAPI endpoints work correctly, including streaming responses.\n   264\u2192- **WebSocket Tests:** Verify real-time communication for audio streaming.\n   265\u2192\n   266\u2192To run the tests:\n   267\u2192\n   268\u21921. **Install Test Dependencies**\n   269\u2192\n   270\u2192   The test dependencies are included in `requirements.txt` (pytest, pytest-cov, pytest-asyncio, pytest-mock, httpx). Make sure they are installed:\n   271\u2192   ```bash\n   272\u2192   pip install -r requirements.txt\n   273\u2192   ```\n   274\u2192\n   275\u21922. **Run Tests**\n   276\u2192\n   277\u2192   ```bash\n   278\u2192   # Run all tests\n   279\u2192   pytest tests/\n   280\u2192\n   281\u2192   # Run tests with verbose output\n   282\u2192   pytest -v tests/\n   283\u2192\n   284\u2192   # Run tests for a specific component\n   285\u2192   pytest tests/test_audio_processor.py\n   286\u2192   ```\n   287\u2192\n   288\u21923. **Test Environment**\n   289\u2192\n   290\u2192   Tests use mocked API clients to avoid actual API calls.     85→class AudioProcessor:
    86→    def __init__(self, target_sample_rate=24000):
    87→        self.target_sample_rate = target_sample_rate
    88→        self.source_sample_rate = 48000  # Most common sample rate for microphones
    89→        
    90→    def process_audio_chunk(self, audio_data):
    91→        # Convert binary audio data to Int16 array
    92→        pcm_data = np.frombuffer(audio_data, dtype=np.int16)
    93→        
    94→        # Convert to float32 for better precision during resampling
    95→        float_data = pcm_data.astype(np.float32) / 32768.0
    96→        
    97→        # Resample from 48kHz to 24kHz
    98→        resampled_data = scipy.signal.resample_poly(
    99→            float_data, 
   100→            self.target_sample_rate, 
   101→            self.source_sample_rate
   102→        )
   103→        
   104→        # Convert back to int16 while preserving amplitude
   105→        resampled_int16 = (resampled_data * 32768.0).clip(-32768, 32767).astype(np.int16)
   106→        return resampled_int16.tobytes()
   107→
   108→    def save_audio_buffer(self, audio_buffer, filename):
   109→        with wave.open(filename, 'wb') as wf:
   110→            wf.setnchannels(1)  # Mono audio
   111→            wf.setsampwidth(2)  # 2 bytes per sample (16-bit)
   112→            wf.setframerate(self.target_sample_rate)
   113→            wf.writeframes(b''.join(audio_buffer))
   114→        logger.info(f"Saved audio buffer to {filename}")
   115→
   116→@app.websocket("/api/v1/ws")
   117→async def websocket_endpoint(websocket: WebSocket):
   118→    logger.info("New WebSocket connection attempt")
   119→    await websocket.accept()
   120→    logger.info("WebSocket connection accepted, starting receive_messages task")
   121→    
   122→    # Add initial status update here
   123→    await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   124→        "type": "status",
   125→        "status": "idle"  # Set initial status to idle (blue)
   126→    }, ensure_ascii=False))
   127→    
   128→    client = None
   129→    audio_processor = AudioProcessor()
   130→    audio_buffer = []
   131→    recording_stopped = asyncio.Event()
   132→    openai_ready = asyncio.Event()
   133→    pending_audio_chunks = []
   134→    clear_on_next_response = False
   135→    is_recording = False
   136→    marker_prefix = "下面是不改变语言的语音识别结果：

"
   137→    max_prefix_deltas = 20
   138→    response_buffer = []
   139→    marker_seen = False
   140→    delta_counter = 0
   141→
   142→    async def emit_text_delta(content: str):
   143→        if content and websocket.client_state == WebSocketState.CONNECTED:
   144→            await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   145→                "type": "text",
   146→                "content": content,
   147→                "isNewResponse": False
   148→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
   149→
   150→    async def flush_buffer(with_warning: bool = False):
   151→        nonlocal response_buffer
   152→        if not response_buffer:
   153→            return
   154→        buffered_text = "".join(response_buffer)
   155→        response_buffer = []
   156→        # Try to remove marker prefix (with or without trailing newlines)
   157→        if buffered_text.startswith(marker_prefix):
   158→            buffered_text = buffered_text[len(marker_prefix):]
   159→        elif buffered_text.startswith(marker_prefix.rstrip('
')):
   160→            # Handle case where prefix doesn't have trailing newlines
   161→            buffered_text = buffered_text[len(marker_prefix.rstrip('
')):].lstrip('
')
   162→        # Also check if prefix appears anywhere in the text
   163→        marker_index = buffered_text.find(marker_prefix)
   164→        if marker_index != -1:
   165→            buffered_text = buffered_text[marker_index + len(marker_prefix):]
   166→        else:
   167→            marker_index = buffered_text.find(marker_prefix.rstrip('
'))
   168→            if marker_index != -1:
   169→                buffered_text = buffered_text[marker_index + len(marker_prefix.rstrip('
')):].lstrip('
')
   170→        if with_warning and not buffered_text:
   171→            logger.warning("Buffered text discarded after removing marker prefix.")
   172→        await emit_text_delta(buffered_text)
   173→    
   174→    async def create_realtime_client(model: str = None) -> OpenAIRealtimeAudioTextClient:
   175→        """Create OpenAI realtime client with given model."""
   176→        selected_model = model or OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL
   177→        logger.info(f"Creating OpenAI client with model: {selected_model}")

   179→    
   180→    async def initialize_realtime_client(model: str = None):

   186→            logger.info("Successfully connected to OpenAI client")
   187→            
   188→            # Register handlers after client is initialized
   189→            client.register_handler("session.updated", lambda data: handle_generic_event("session.updated", data))
   190→            client.register_handler("input_audio_buffer.cleared", lambda data: handle_generic_event("input_audio_buffer.cleared", data))
   191→            client.register_handler("input_audio_buffer.speech_started", lambda data: handle_generic_event("input_audio_buffer.speech_started", data))
   192→            client.register_handler("rate_limits.updated", lambda data: handle_generic_event("rate_limits.updated", data))

   200→            client.register_handler("error", lambda data: handle_error(data))
   201→            client.register_handler("response.text.delta", lambda data: handle_text_delta(data))
   202→            # GA: response.text.delta → response.output_text.delta
   203→            client.register_handler("response.output_text.delta", lambda data: handle_text_delta(data))
   204→            client.register_handler("response.created", lambda data: handle_response_created(data))
   205→            client.register_handler("input_audio_buffer.speech_stopped", lambda data: handle_generic_event("input_audio_buffer.speech_stopped", data))
   206→            client.register_handler("input_audio_buffer.committed", lambda data: handle_generic_event("input_audio_buffer.committed", data))
   207→            client.register_handler("conversation.item.added", lambda data: handle_generic_event("conversation.item.added", data))
   208→            client.register_handler("conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.completed", lambda data: handle_generic_event("conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.completed", data))
   209→            client.register_handler("response.output_audio.done", lambda data: handle_generic_event("response.output_audio.done", data))
   210→            client.register_handler("ping", lambda data: handle_generic_event("ping", data))
   211→            
   212→            openai_ready.set()  # Set ready flag after successful initialization
   213→            await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   214→                "type": "status",
   215→                "status": "connected"
   216→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
   217→            return True
   218→        except Exception as e:
   219→            logger.error(f"Failed to connect to OpenAI client: {e}")
   220→            openai_ready.clear()  # Ensure flag is cleared on failure
   221→            await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   222→                "type": "error",
   223→                "content": "Failed to initialize OpenAI connection"
   224→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
   225→            return False
   226→
   227→    # Move the handler definitions here (before initialize_realtime_client)
   228→    async def handle_text_delta(data):
   229→        nonlocal response_buffer, marker_seen, delta_counter
   230→        try:
   231→            if websocket.client_state != WebSocketState.CONNECTED:
   232→                logger.warning("WebSocket not connected, ignoring text delta")
   233→                return
   234→
   235→            delta = data.get("delta", "")
   236→            logger.debug(f"Received text delta: {repr(delta[:50])} (marker_seen={marker_seen}, buffer_size={len(response_buffer)}, delta_counter={delta_counter})")
   237→
   238→            if marker_seen:
   239→                if delta:
   240→                    await emit_text_delta(delta)
   241→                    logger.debug(f"Handled response.text.delta (passthrough): {repr(delta[:50])}")
   242→                return
   243→
   244→            if delta:
   245→                response_buffer.append(delta)
   246→                delta_counter += 1
   247→
   248→            joined = "".join(response_buffer)
   249→            # Try to find marker prefix (with or without newlines)
   250→            marker_index = joined.find(marker_prefix)
   251→            # Also try without the trailing newlines in case x.ai returns differently
   252→            if marker_index == -1:
   253→                marker_prefix_no_newline = marker_prefix.rstrip('
')
   254→                marker_index = joined.find(marker_prefix_no_newline)
   255→                if marker_index != -1:
   256→                    # Found prefix without trailing newlines, skip past it
   257→                    marker_seen = True
   258→                    remaining = joined[marker_index + len(marker_prefix_no_newline):].lstrip('
')
   259→                    response_buffer = []
   260→                    if remaining:
   261→                        await emit_text_delta(remaining)
   262→                    logger.info(f"Handled response.text.delta (marker detected without newline), emitted: {repr(remaining[:50])}")
   263→                    return
   264→
   265→            if marker_index != -1:
   266→                marker_seen = True
   267→                remaining = joined[marker_index + len(marker_prefix):]
   268→                response_buffer = []
   269→                await emit_text_delta(remaining)
   270→                logger.info(f"Handled response.text.delta (marker detected), emitted: {repr(remaining[:50])}")
   271→                return
   272→
   273→            if delta_counter >= max_prefix_deltas:
   274→                marker_seen = True
   275→                await flush_buffer(with_warning=True)
   276→                logger.warning("Marker prefix not detected after max deltas; emitted buffered text.")
   277→            else:
   278→                logger.debug(f"Handled response.text.delta (buffering), total buffer length: {len(joined)}")
   279→        except Exception as e:
   280→            logger.error(f"Error in handle_text_delta: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   281→
   282→    async def handle_response_created(data):
   283→        # Only clear UI on the first response after an explicit Start from the user
   284→        nonlocal clear_on_next_response, response_buffer, marker_seen, delta_counter
   285→        response_buffer = []
   286→        marker_seen = False
   287→        delta_counter = 0
   288→        logger.info(f"Handled response.created, clearing buffer and resetting marker state")
   289→        if clear_on_next_response:
   290→            await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   291→                "type": "text",
   292→                "content": "",
   293→                "isNewResponse": True
   294→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
   295→            clear_on_next_response = False
   296→        logger.info("Handled response.created")
   297→
   298→    async def handle_error(data):
   299→        error_msg = data.get("error", {}).get("message", "Unknown error")
   300→        logger.error(f"OpenAI error: {error_msg}")
   301→        await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   302→            "type": "error",
   303→            "content": error_msg
   304→        }, ensure_ascii=False))
   305→        # Ensure clients exit generating state even if OpenAI aborts the turn
   306→        await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   307→            "type": "status",
   308→            "status": "idle"
   309→        }, ensure_ascii=False))
   310→        logger.info("Handled error message from OpenAI")
   311→
   312→    async def handle_response_done(data):
   313→        nonlocal client, response_buffer, marker_seen
   314→        logger.info(f"Handled response.done (marker_seen={marker_seen}, buffer_size={len(response_buffer)})")
   315→        if not marker_seen and response_buffer:
   316→            logger.info("Flushing remaining buffer content")
   317→            await flush_buffer()
   318→            marker_seen = True
   319→        
   320→        recording_stopped.set()
   321→        
   322→        # Update frontend status to idle
   323→        try:
   324→            await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   325→                "type": "status",
   326→                "status": "idle"
   327→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
   328→        except Exception as e:
   329→            logger.error(f"Error sending status after response done: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   330→        
   331→        # Close the OpenAI client connection (not the user WebSocket)
   332→        # The user WebSocket should remain open for the next request
   333→        if client:
   334→            logger.info("Response completed, closing OpenAI client connection")
   335→            try:
   336→                await client.close()
   337→                client = None
   338→                openai_ready.clear()
   339→            except Exception as e:
   340→                logger.error(f"Error closing OpenAI client: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   341→
   342→    async def handle_generic_event(event_type, data):
   343→        logger.info(f"Handled {event_type} with data: {json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False)}")
   344→
   345→    # Create a queue to handle incoming audio chunks
   346→    audio_queue = asyncio.Queue()
   347→
   348→    async def receive_messages():
   349→        nonlocal client
   350→        logger.info("receive_messages task started")
   351→        
   352→        try:
   353→            while True:
   354→                if websocket.client_state == WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED:
   355→                    logger.info("WebSocket client disconnected")
   356→                    openai_ready.clear()
   357→                    break
   358→                    
   359→                try:
   360→                    # Add timeout to prevent infinite waiting
   361→                    logger.info("Waiting for message from client (timeout=30s)...")
   362→                    data = await asyncio.wait_for(websocket.receive(), timeout=30.0)
   363→                    logger.info(f"Received data from client: {list(data.keys())}")
   364→                except asyncio.CancelledError:
   365→                    logger.info("Receive messages task cancelled")
   366→                    raise
   367→                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   368→                    logger.debug("No message received for 30 seconds")
   369→                    continue
   370→                except Exception as e:
   371→                    logger.error(f"Error receiving message: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   372→                    break
   373→                
   374→                if "bytes" in data:
   375→                    processed_audio = audio_processor.process_audio_chunk(data["bytes"])
   376→                    if not openai_ready.is_set():
   377→                        logger.debug("OpenAI not ready, buffering audio chunk")
   378→                        pending_audio_chunks.append(processed_audio)
   379→                    elif client and is_recording:
   380→                        await client.send_audio(processed_audio)
   381→                        await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   382→                            "type": "status",
   383→                            "status": "connected"
   384→                        }, ensure_ascii=False))
   385→                        logger.debug(f"Sent audio chunk, size: {len(processed_audio)} bytes")
   386→                    else:
   387→                        logger.warning("Received audio but client is not initialized")
   388→                            
   389→                elif "text" in data:
   390→                    msg = json.loads(data["text"])
   391→                    logger.info(f"Received message from client: {msg.get('type')}")
   392→                    
   393→                    if msg.get("type") == "start_recording":
   394→                        logger.info("Processing start_recording request")
   395→                        
   396→                        # Update status to connecting while initializing realtime client
   397→                        await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   398→                            "type": "status",
   399→                            "status": "connecting"
   400→                        }, ensure_ascii=False))
   401→                        model = msg.get("model")
   402→                        logger.info(f"Received start_recording: model={model}")
   403→                        if not await initialize_realtime_client(model=model):
   404→                            continue
   405→                        recording_stopped.clear()
   406→                        pending_audio_chunks.clear()
   407→                        # Immediately clear transcript for a new client-initiated request
   408→                        await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   409→                            "type": "text",
   410→                            "content": "",
   411→                            "isNewResponse": True
   412→                        }, ensure_ascii=False))
   413→                        clear_on_next_response = False
   414→                        is_recording = True
   415→                        
   416→                        # Send any buffered chunks
   417→                        if pending_audio_chunks and client:
   418→                            logger.info(f"Sending {len(pending_audio_chunks)} buffered chunks")
   419→                            for chunk in pending_audio_chunks:
   420→                                await client.send_audio(chunk)
   421→                            pending_audio_chunks.clear()
   422→                        
   423→                    elif msg.get("type") == "stop_recording":
   424→                        # On explicit Stop, force-commit and force-create a response, then wait for completion.
   425→                        if client:
   426→                            # Immediately stop accepting further audio for this turn
   427→                            is_recording = False
   428→                            try:
   429→                                await client.commit_audio()
   430→                                logger.info("Audio committed, starting response...")
   431→                                await client.start_response(PROMPTS['paraphrase-gpt-realtime-enhanced'])
   432→                                logger.info("Response started successfully")
   433→                            except Exception as e:
   434→                                logger.error(f"Error committing/starting response on stop: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   435→                                # If we fail to kick off a response, surface that we're no longer recording
   436→                                await websocket.send_text(json.dumps({
   437→                                    "type": "status",
   438→                                    "status": "idle"
   439→                                }, ensure_ascii=False))
   440→                                continue
   441→                            # Wait until the response is finished
   442→                            await recording_stopped.wait()
   443→                
   444→        finally:
   445→            # Cleanup when the loop exits
   446→            if client:
   447→                try:
   448→                    await client.close()
   449→                except Exception as e:
   450→                    logger.error(f"Error closing client in receive_messages: {str(e)}")
   451→            logger.info("Receive messages loop ended")
   452→
   453→    async def send_audio_messages():
   454→        try:
   455→            while True:
   456→                
   457→                try:
   458→                    processed_audio = await audio_queue.get()
   459→                    if processed_audio is None:
   460→                        break
   461→                    
   462→                    # Add validation
   463→                    if len(processed_audio) == 0:
   464→                        logger.warning("Empty audio chunk received, skipping")
   465→                        continue

   467→                    # Append the processed audio to the buffer
   468→                    audio_buffer.append(processed_audio)
   469→

   471→                    logger.info(f"Audio chunk sent to OpenAI client, size: {len(processed_audio)} bytes")
   472→                    
   473→                except asyncio.CancelledError:
   474→                    logger.info("Send audio messages task cancelled")
   475→                    raise
   476→                except Exception as e:
   477→                    logger.error(f"Error in send_audio_messages: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
   478→                    break

   480→            logger.info("Send audio messages task cancelled")
   481→            raise
   482→
   483→        # After processing all audio, set the event
   484→        recording_stopped.set()

   486→    # Start concurrent tasks for receiving and sending
   487→    receive_task = asyncio.create_task(receive_messages())
   488→    send_task = asyncio.create_task(send_audio_messages())
   489→
   490→    try:
   491→        # Wait for both tasks to complete
   492→        await asyncio.gather(receive_task, send_task)
   493→    except Exception as e:
   494→        logger.error(f"Error in WebSocket connection: {e}", exc_info=True)
   495→    finally:
   496→        # Cancel background tasks before cleanup

   498→        send_task.cancel()
   499→        
   500→        # Wait for tasks to be cancelled (with timeout)

   503→        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   504→            logger.warning("Tasks did not cancel within timeout")
   505→        except Exception as e:

   507→        
   508→        if client:

   513→            except RuntimeError as e:
   514→                logger.warning(f"Ignoring error during websocket close: {e}")
   515→        logger.info("WebSocket connection closed for /api/v1/ws")
   516→
   517→@app.post(

     1→import websockets

     4→import logging

     7→import asyncio
     8→import os
     9→from prompts import PROMPTS
    10→from config import OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL
    11→from realtime_client_base import RealtimeClientBase
    12→
    13→logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    14→logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    15→
    16→class OpenAIRealtimeAudioTextClient(RealtimeClientBase):
    17→    def __init__(self, api_key: str, model: str = OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL):
    18→        super().__init__(api_key)
    19→        self.model = model
    20→        self.base_url = "wss://api.openai.com/v1/realtime"
    21→        self.last_audio_time = None 
    22→        self.auto_commit_interval = 5
    23→        
    24→    async def connect(self, modalities: List[str] = ["text"], session_mode: str = "conversation"):
    25→        """Connect to OpenAI's realtime API and configure the session"""
    26→        headers = {
    27→            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
    28→        }
    29→
    30→        # Support both websockets param names across versions: extra_headers (older) and additional_headers (newer)
    31→        try:
    32→            self.ws = await websockets.connect(
    33→                f"{self.base_url}?model={self.model}",
    34→                extra_headers=headers,
    35→            )
    36→        except TypeError:
    37→            # Fallback for newer versions where the kwarg is 'additional_headers'
    38→            self.ws = await websockets.connect(
    39→                f"{self.base_url}?model={self.model}",
    40→                additional_headers=headers,
    41→            )
    42→        
    43→        # Wait for session creation
    44→        response = await self.ws.recv()
    45→        response_data = json.loads(response)
    46→        if response_data["type"] == "session.created":
    47→            self.session_id = response_data["session"]["id"]
    48→            logger.info(f"Session created with ID: {self.session_id}")
    49→            
    50→            session_config_payload = {
    51→                "type": "realtime" if session_mode == "conversation" else "transcription",
    52→                "output_modalities": modalities,
    53→                "audio": {
    54→                    "input": {
    55→                        "format": {"type": "audio/pcm", "rate": 24000},
    56→                        "transcription": {"model": "gpt-4o-transcribe"},
    57→                        "turn_detection": None,
    58→                    }
    59→                },
    60→            }
    61→
    62→            if session_mode == "transcription":
    63→                logger.info("Configuring session for transcription mode.")
    64→            else:
    65→                session_config_payload["instructions"] = PROMPTS['paraphrase-gpt-realtime-enhanced']
    66→                logger.info("Configuring session for conversation mode with transcription and no turn detection.")
    67→
    68→            # Configure session
    69→            await self.ws.send(json.dumps({
    70→                "type": "session.update",
    71→                "session": session_config_payload
    72→            }, ensure_ascii=False))
    73→        
    74→        # Register the default handler
    75→        self.register_handler("default", self.default_handler)
    76→        
    77→        # Start the receiver coroutine
    78→        self.receive_task = asyncio.create_task(self.receive_messages())
    79→
    80→    
    81→    async def send_instructions_audio(self):
    82→        """Send the instructions.wav file as audio input to be appended to current buffer"""
    83→        instructions_path = "instructions.wav"
    84→        if not os.path.exists(instructions_path):
    85→            logger.warning(f"Instructions audio file not found: {instructions_path}")
    86→            return
    87→            
    88→        try:
    89→            with open(instructions_path, "rb") as f:
    90→                audio_data = f.read()
    91→            
    92→            # Send the instructions audio to the buffer (appends to existing user audio)
    93→            await self.send_audio(audio_data)
    94→            logger.info("Sent instructions audio to OpenAI buffer (appended to user audio)")
    95→            
    96→        except Exception as e:
    97→            logger.error(f"Error sending instructions audio: {e}")
    98→    
    99→    async def receive_messages(self):
   100→        try:
   101→            async for message in self.ws:
   102→                data = json.loads(message)
   103→                message_type = data.get("type", "default")
   104→                handler = self.handlers.get(message_type, self.handlers.get("default"))
   105→                if handler:
   106→                    await handler(data)
   107→                else:
   108→                    logger.warning(f"No handler for message type: {message_type}")
   109→        except websockets.exceptions.ConnectionClosed as e:
   110→            logger.error(f"OpenAI WebSocket connection closed: {e}")
   111→        except Exception as e:
   112→            logger.error(f"Error in receive_messages: {e}", exc_info=True)
   113→    
   114→    async def default_handler(self, data: dict):
   115→        """Override default handler for OpenAI-specific logging"""
   116→        message_type = data.get("type", "unknown")
   117→        logger.warning(f"Unhandled message type received from OpenAI: {message_type}")
   118→    
   119→    async def send_audio(self, audio_data: bytes):
   120→        if self._is_ws_open():
   121→            await self.ws.send(json.dumps({
   122→                "type": "input_audio_buffer.append",
   123→                "audio": base64.b64encode(audio_data).decode('utf-8')
   124→            }))
   125→        else:
   126→            logger.error("WebSocket is not open. Cannot send audio.")
   127→    
   128→    async def commit_audio(self):
   129→        """Commit the audio buffer and notify OpenAI"""
   130→        if self._is_ws_open():
   131→            commit_message = json.dumps({"type": "input_audio_buffer.commit"})
   132→            await self.ws.send(commit_message)
   133→            logger.info("Sent input_audio_buffer.commit message to OpenAI")
   134→            # No recv call here. The receive_messages coroutine handles incoming messages.
   135→        else:
   136→            logger.error("WebSocket is not open. Cannot commit audio.")
   137→    
   138→    async def clear_audio_buffer(self):
   139→        """Clear the audio buffer"""
   140→        if self._is_ws_open():
   141→            clear_message = json.dumps({"type": "input_audio_buffer.clear"})
   142→            await self.ws.send(clear_message)
   143→            logger.info("Sent input_audio_buffer.clear message to OpenAI")
   144→        else:
   145→            logger.error("WebSocket is not open. Cannot clear audio buffer.")
   146→    
   147→    async def start_response(self, instructions: str):
   148→        """Start a new response with given instructions"""
   149→        if self._is_ws_open():
   150→            await self.ws.send(json.dumps({
   151→                "type": "response.create",
   152→                "response": {
   153→                    "output_modalities": ["text"],
   154→                    "instructions": instructions
   155→                }
   156→            }))
   157→            logger.info(f"Started response with instructions: {instructions}")
   158→        else:
   159→            logger.error("WebSocket is not open. Cannot start response.")
   160→    
   161→    async def close(self):
   162→        """Close the WebSocket connection"""
   163→        if self.ws:
   164→            await self.ws.close()
   165→            logger.info("Closed OpenAI WebSocket connection")
   166→        if self.receive_task:
   167→            self.receive_task.cancel()
   168→            try:
   169→                await self.receive_task
   170→            except asyncio.CancelledError:
   171→                pass
   172→

    40→async function copyToClipboard(text, button) {
    41→    if (!text) return;
    42→    try {
    43→        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    44→        showCopiedFeedback(button, 'Copied!');
    45→    } catch (err) {
    46→        console.error('Clipboard copy failed:', err);
    47→        // alert('Clipboard copy failed: ' + err.message);
    48→        // We don't show this message because it's not accurate. We could still write to the clipboard in this case.
    49→    }
    50→}
    51→
    52→function showCopiedFeedback(button, message) {
    53→    if (!button) return;
    54→    const originalText = button.textContent;
    55→    button.textContent = message;
    56→    setTimeout(() => {
    57→        button.textContent = originalText;
    58→    }, 2000);
    59→}
    60→
    61→// Timer functions
    62→function startTimer() {
    63→    clearInterval(timerInterval);
    64→    document.getElementById('timer').textContent = '00:00';
    65→    startTime = Date.now();
    66→    timerInterval = setInterval(() => {
    67→        const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;
    68→        const minutes = Math.floor(elapsed / 60000);
    69→        const seconds = Math.floor((elapsed % 60000) / 1000);
    70→        document.getElementById('timer').textContent = 
    71→            `${minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
    72→    }, 1000);
    73→}
    74→
    75→function stopTimer() {
    76→    clearInterval(timerInterval);
    77→}

    79→// IndexedDB initialization
    80→async function initIndexedDB() {
    81→    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    82→        const request = indexedDB.open('brainwave-replay', 1);
    83→        
    84→        request.onerror = () => {
    85→            console.warn('IndexedDB not available, replay disabled');
    86→            storageAvailable = false;
    87→            if (replayButton) {
    88→                replayButton.disabled = true;
    89→                replayButton.title = 'Local storage not available';
    90→            }
    91→            resolve(false);
    92→        };
    93→        
    94→        request.onsuccess = () => {
    95→            db = request.result;
    96→            
    97→            // Check if required object stores exist
    98→            if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('sessions') || !db.objectStoreNames.contains('chunks')) {
    99→                // Close and delete the database, then reopen to trigger onupgradeneeded
   100→                db.close();
   101→                const deleteRequest = indexedDB.deleteDatabase('brainwave-replay');
   102→                deleteRequest.onsuccess = () => {
   103→                    // Reopen database - this will trigger onupgradeneeded
   104→                    const reopenRequest = indexedDB.open('brainwave-replay', 1);
   105→                    reopenRequest.onsuccess = () => {
   106→                        db = reopenRequest.result;
   107→                        storageAvailable = true;
   108→                        if (replayButton) {
   109→                            replayButton.disabled = false;
   110→                        }
   111→                        updateReplayButtonState();
   112→                        resolve(true);
   113→                    };
   114→                    reopenRequest.onerror = () => {
   115→                        console.warn('Failed to reopen IndexedDB after cleanup');
   116→                        storageAvailable = false;
   117→                        if (replayButton) {
   118→                            replayButton.disabled = true;
   119→                            replayButton.title = 'Local storage not available';
   120→                        }

   174→            }

   177→}
   178→
   179→// Audio processing
   180→function createAudioProcessor() {
   181→    processor = audioContext.createScriptProcessor(4096, 1, 1);
   182→    processor.onaudioprocess = async (e) => {
   183→        // Allow processing if recording OR if stopping (to capture final audio)
   184→        if (!isRecording && !isStopping) return;
   185→        
   186→        const inputData = e.inputBuffer.getChannelData(0);
   187→        const pcmData = new Int16Array(inputData.length);
   188→        
   189→        for (let i = 0; i < inputData.length; i++) {
   190→            pcmData[i] = Math.max(-32768, Math.min(32767, Math.floor(inputData[i] * 32767)));
   191→        }
   192→        
   193→        const combinedBuffer = new Int16Array(audioBuffer.length + pcmData.length);
   194→        combinedBuffer.set(audioBuffer);
   195→        combinedBuffer.set(pcmData, audioBuffer.length);
   196→        audioBuffer = combinedBuffer;
   197→        
   198→        if (audioBuffer.length >= 24000) {
   199→            const sendBuffer = audioBuffer.slice(0, 24000);
   200→            audioBuffer = audioBuffer.slice(24000);
   201→            
   202→            if (ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   203→                ws.send(sendBuffer.buffer);
   204→                
   205→                // Store chunk in IndexedDB
   206→                if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId && sessionStartTime) {
   207→                    const deltaMs = performance.now() - sessionStartTime;
   208→                    await appendChunk(currentSessionId, {
   209→                        seq: chunkSeq++,
   210→                        deltaMs: deltaMs,
   211→                        kind: 'audio',
   212→                        payload: sendBuffer.buffer,
   213→                        byteLength: sendBuffer.byteLength
   214→                    });
   215→                }
   216→            }
   217→        }
   218→    };
   219→    return processor;
   220→}
   221→
   222→async function initAudio(stream) {
   223→    console.log('Initializing AudioContext...');
   224→    // Clean up existing audio context if any
   225→    if (audioContext && audioContext.state !== 'closed') {
   226→        try {
   227→            await audioContext.close();
   228→        } catch (e) {
   229→            console.warn('Error closing existing audio context:', e);
   230→        }
   231→    }
   232→    
   233→    try {
   234→        audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
   235→        source = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
   236→        processor = createAudioProcessor();
   237→        source.connect(processor);
   238→        processor.connect(audioContext.destination);
   239→        
   240→        if (audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
   241→            await audioContext.resume();
   242→        }
   243→    } catch (e) {
   244→        console.error('initAudio failed:', e);
   245→        throw e;
   246→    }
   247→}
   248→
   249→function cleanupAudioResources() {
   250→    // Stop all tracks in the stream
   251→    if (stream) {
   252→        stream.getTracks().forEach(track => {
   253→            track.stop();
   254→        });
   255→        stream = null;
   256→    }
   257→    
   258→    // Close audio context
   259→    if (audioContext && audioContext.state !== 'closed') {
   260→        audioContext.close().catch(e => {
   261→            console.warn('Error closing audio context:', e);
   262→        });
   263→        audioContext = null;
   264→    }
   265→    
   266→    source = null;
   267→    processor = null;
   268→    streamInitialized = false;
   269→}
   270→
   271→// WebSocket handling
   272→function updateConnectionStatus(status) {
   273→    const statusDot = document.getElementById('connectionStatus');
   274→    statusDot.classList.remove('connected', 'connecting', 'idle');
   275→    
   276→    switch (status) {
   277→        case 'connected':  // OpenAI is connected and ready
   278→            statusDot.classList.add('connected');
   279→            statusDot.style.backgroundColor = '#34C759';  // Green
   280→            break;
   281→        case 'connecting':  // Establishing OpenAI connection
   282→            statusDot.classList.add('connecting');
   283→            statusDot.style.backgroundColor = '#FF9500';  // Orange
   284→            break;
   285→        case 'idle':  // Client connected, OpenAI not connected
   286→            statusDot.classList.add('idle');
   287→            statusDot.style.backgroundColor = '#007AFF';  // Blue
   288→            break;
   289→        default:  // Disconnected
   290→            statusDot.style.backgroundColor = '#FF3B30';  // Red
   291→    }
   292→}

    47→        genai_model = genai.GenerativeModel(model_name)

    49→        return response.text

    51→class GPTProcessor(LLMProcessor):
    52→    def __init__(self):
    53→        if not os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"):
    54→            raise ValueError("OpenAI API key not found in environment variables")
    55→        self.async_client = AsyncOpenAI(api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))
    56→        self.sync_client = OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))
    57→        self.default_model = "gpt-4"
    58→
    59→    async def process_text(self, text: str, prompt: str, model: Optional[str] = None) -> AsyncGenerator[str, None]:
    60→        all_prompt = f"{prompt}

{text}"
    61→        model_name = model or self.default_model
    62→        logger.info(f"Using model: {model_name} for processing")
    63→        logger.debug(f"Prompt (length={len(all_prompt)} chars)")
    64→        response = await self.async_client.chat.completions.create(
    65→            model=model_name,
    66→            messages=[
    67→                {"role": "user", "content": all_prompt}
    68→            ],
    69→            stream=True
    70→        )
    71→        async for chunk in response:
    72→            if chunk.choices and chunk.choices[0].delta.content:
    73→                yield chunk.choices[0].delta.content
    74→
    75→    def process_text_sync(self, text: str, prompt: str, model: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
    76→        all_prompt = f"{prompt}

{text}"
    77→        model_name = model or self.default_model
    78→        logger.info(f"Using model: {model_name} for sync processing")
    79→        logger.debug(f"Prompt (length={len(all_prompt)} chars)")
    80→        response = self.sync_client.chat.completions.create(
    81→            model=model_name,
    82→            messages=[
    83→                {"role": "user", "content": all_prompt}
    84→            ]
    85→        )
    86→        return response.choices[0].message.content
    87→
    88→def get_llm_processor(model: str) -> LLMProcessor:
    89→    model = model.lower()
    90→    if model.startswith(('gemini', 'gemini-')):
    91→        return GeminiProcessor(default_model=model)

     1→"""
     2→Abstract base class for realtime audio-text clients.
     3→Provides a common interface for different providers (OpenAI, x.ai, etc.)
     4→"""
     5→from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
     6→from typing import Callable, Dict, List
     7→import asyncio
     8→import logging
     9→
    10→logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    11→
    12→
    13→class RealtimeClientBase(ABC):
    14→    """Abstract base class for realtime audio-text API clients"""
    15→    
    16→    def __init__(self, api_key: str):
    17→        """
    18→        Initialize the realtime client.
    19→        
    20→        Args:
    21→            api_key: API key for the provider
    22→        """
    23→        self.api_key = api_key
    24→        self.ws = None
    25→        self.session_id = None
    26→        self.receive_task = None
    27→        self.handlers: Dict[str, Callable[[dict], asyncio.Future]] = {}
    28→        self.queue = asyncio.Queue()
    29→    
    30→    @abstractmethod
    31→    async def connect(self, modalities: List[str] = None, session_mode: str = "conversation"):
    32→        """
    33→        Connect to the realtime API and configure the session.
    34→        
    35→        Args:
    36→            modalities: List of modalities to use (e.g., ["text", "audio"])
    37→            session_mode: Mode for the session ("conversation" or "transcription")
    38→        """
    39→        pass
    40→    
    41→    @abstractmethod
    42→    async def send_audio(self, audio_data: bytes):
    43→        """
    44→        Send audio data to the API.
    45→        
    46→        Args:
    47→            audio_data: Raw PCM16 audio bytes
    48→        """
    49→        pass
    50→    
    51→    @abstractmethod
    52→    async def commit_audio(self):
    53→        """Commit the audio buffer."""
    54→        pass
    55→    
    56→    @abstractmethod
    57→    async def clear_audio_buffer(self):
    58→        """Clear the audio buffer."""
    59→        pass
    60→    
    61→    @abstractmethod
    62→    async def close(self):
    63→        """Close the WebSocket connection and cleanup."""
    64→        pass
    65→    
    66→    def register_handler(self, message_type: str, handler: Callable[[dict], asyncio.Future]):
    67→        """
    68→        Register a handler for a specific message type.
    69→        
    70→        Args:
    71→            message_type: Type of message to handle
    72→            handler: Async function that processes the message
    73→        """
    74→        self.handlers[message_type] = handler
    75→    
    76→    def _is_ws_open(self) -> bool:
    77→        """
    78→        Check if WebSocket connection is open.
    79→        Compatibility check for different websockets versions.
    80→        
    81→        Returns:
    82→            True if connection is open, False otherwise
    83→        """
    84→        if not self.ws:
    85→            return False
    86→        # Prefer 'closed' if available (newer versions)
    87→        if hasattr(self.ws, "closed"):
    88→            try:
    89→                return not bool(self.ws.closed)
    90→            except Exception:
    91→                pass
    92→        # Fallback to 'open' (older versions)
    93→        if hasattr(self.ws, "open"):
    94→            try:
    95→                return bool(self.ws.open)
    96→            except Exception:
    97→                pass
    98→        # If neither attribute is reliable, assume open if object exists
    99→        return True
   100→    
   101→    async def default_handler(self, data: dict):
   102→        """
   103→        Default handler for unhandled message types.
   104→        Override in subclasses if needed.
   105→        
   106→        Args:
   107→            data: Message data
   108→        """
   109→        message_type = data.get("type", "unknown")
   110→        logger.warning(f"Unhandled message type received: {message_type}")

   311→    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
   312→        const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
   313→        switch (data.type) {
   314→            case 'status':
   315→                updateConnectionStatus(data.status);
   316→                // Stop timer when not actively recording/generating
   317→                if (data.status === 'idle' || data.status === 'generating') {
   318→                    stopTimer();
   319→                }
   320→                if (data.status === 'idle') {
   321→                    copyToClipboard(transcript.value, copyButton);
   322→                    // Update replay button state when status becomes idle
   323→                    updateReplayButtonState();
   324→                }
   325→                break;
   326→            case 'text':
   327→                if (data.isNewResponse) {
   328→                    transcript.value = data.content;
   329→                    stopTimer();
   330→                } else {
   331→                    transcript.value += data.content;
   332→                }
   333→                transcript.scrollTop = transcript.scrollHeight;
   334→                break;
   335→            case 'error':
   336→                alert(data.content);
   337→                updateConnectionStatus('idle');
   338→                updateReplayButtonState();
   339→                break;
   340→        }
   341→    };
   342→

   344→        wsConnected = false;
