   357→// IndexedDB helpers
   358→async function createSession() {
   359→    if (!db) return null;
   360→    
   361→    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   362→        const transaction = db.transaction(['sessions'], 'readwrite');
   363→        const store = transaction.objectStore('sessions');
   364→        const session = {
   365→            createdAt: new Date(),
   366→            status: 'recording',
   367→            sampleRate: 24000,
   368→            channelCount: 1,
   369→            durationMs: 0
   370→        };
   371→        
   372→        const request = store.add(session);
   373→        request.onsuccess = () => {
   374→            currentSessionId = request.result;
   375→            sessionStartTime = performance.now();
   376→            chunkSeq = 0;
   377→            
   378→            // Store start event
   379→            appendChunk(currentSessionId, {
   380→                seq: 0,
   381→                deltaMs: 0,
   382→                kind: 'start',
   383→                payload: null,
   384→                byteLength: 0
   385→            });
   386→            
   387→            resolve(currentSessionId);
   388→        };
   389→        request.onerror = () => reject(request.error);
   390→    });
   391→}
   392→
   393→async function appendChunk(sessionId, chunk) {
   394→    if (!db || !sessionId) return;
   395→    
   396→    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   397→        const transaction = db.transaction(['chunks'], 'readwrite');
   398→        const store = transaction.objectStore('chunks');
   399→        const chunkData = {
   400→            sessionId: sessionId,
   401→            seq: chunk.seq,
   402→            deltaMs: chunk.deltaMs,
   403→            kind: chunk.kind,
   404→            payload: chunk.payload,
   405→            byteLength: chunk.byteLength
   406→        };
   407→        
   408→        const request = store.add(chunkData);
   409→        request.onsuccess = () => resolve();
   410→        request.onerror = () => {
   411→            console.warn('Failed to store chunk:', request.error);
   412→            resolve(); // Don't fail recording if storage fails
   413→        };
   414→    });
   415→}
   416→
   417→async function completeSession(sessionId, durationMs) {
   418→    if (!db || !sessionId) return;
   419→    
   420→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   421→        const transaction = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   422→        const sessionsStore = transaction.objectStore('sessions');
   423→        const chunksStore = transaction.objectStore('chunks');
   424→        
   425→        // Update session status
   426→        const getRequest = sessionsStore.get(sessionId);
   427→        getRequest.onsuccess = () => {
   428→            const session = getRequest.result;
   429→            session.status = 'completed';
   430→            session.durationMs = durationMs;
   431→            sessionsStore.put(session);
   432→            
   433→            // Store stop event
   434→            chunksStore.add({
   435→                sessionId: sessionId,
   436→                seq: chunkSeq++,
   437→                deltaMs: durationMs,
   438→                kind: 'stop',
   439→                payload: null,
   440→                byteLength: 0
   441→            });
   442→            
   443→            // Enforce quota
   444→            enforceQuota({ maxSessions: 5, maxBytes: 100 * 1024 * 1024 });
   445→            
   446→            resolve();
   447→        };
   448→        getRequest.onerror = () => resolve();
   449→    });
   450→}
   451→
   452→async function enforceQuota({ maxSessions, maxBytes }) {
   453→    if (!db) return;
   454→    
   455→    const transaction = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   456→    const sessionsStore = transaction.objectStore('sessions');
   457→    const chunksStore = transaction.objectStore('chunks');
   458→    const index = sessionsStore.index('createdAt');
   459→    
   460→    const sessions = [];
   461→    index.openCursor().onsuccess = (event) => {
   462→        const cursor = event.target.result;
   463→        if (cursor) {
   464→            sessions.push(cursor.value);
   465→            cursor.continue();
   466→        } else {
   467→            // Sort by creation time (oldest first)
   468→            sessions.sort((a, b) => a.createdAt - b.createdAt);
   469→            
   470→            // Delete oldest sessions if over limit
   471→            while (sessions.length > maxSessions) {
   472→                const session = sessions.shift();
   473→                deleteSession(session.id);
   474→            }
   475→        }
   476→    };
   477→}
   478→
   479→async function deleteSession(sessionId) {
   480→    if (!db) return;
   481→    
   482→    const transaction = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   483→    const sessionsStore = transaction.objectStore('sessions');
   484→    const chunksStore = transaction.objectStore('chunks');
   485→    const index = chunksStore.index('sessionId');
   486→    
   487→    // Delete all chunks for this session
   488→    index.openKeyCursor(IDBKeyRange.only(sessionId)).onsuccess = (event) => {
   489→        const cursor = event.target.result;
   490→        if (cursor) {
   491→            chunksStore.delete(cursor.primaryKey);
   492→            cursor.continue();
   493→        }
   494→    };
   495→    
   496→    // Delete session
   497→    sessionsStore.delete(sessionId);
   498→}
   499→
   500→async function getLatestCompletedSession() {
   501→    if (!db) return null;
   502→    
   503→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   504→        const transaction = db.transaction(['sessions'], 'readonly');
   505→        const store = transaction.objectStore('sessions');
   506→        const index = store.index('status');
   507→        const request = index.getAll('completed');
   508→        
   509→        request.onsuccess = () => {
   510→            const sessions = request.result;
   511→            if (sessions.length === 0) {
   512→                resolve(null);
   513→                return;
   514→            }
   515→            
   516→            // Sort by creation time (newest first)
   517→            sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt - a.createdAt);
   518→            resolve(sessions[0]);
   519→        };
   520→        request.onerror = () => resolve(null);
   521→    });
   522→}
   523→
   524→async function getSessionChunks(sessionId) {
   525→    if (!db || !sessionId) return [];
   526→    
   527→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   528→        const transaction = db.transaction(['chunks'], 'readonly');
   529→        const store = transaction.objectStore('chunks');
   530→        const index = store.index('sessionId');
   531→        const request = index.getAll(sessionId);
   532→        
   533→        request.onsuccess = () => {
   534→            const chunks = request.result;
   535→            chunks.sort((a, b) => a.seq - b.seq);
   536→            resolve(chunks);
   537→        };
   538→        request.onerror = () => resolve([]);
   539→    });
   540→}
   541→
   542→// Recording control
   543→async function startRecording() {
   544→    if (isRecording || isReplaying) return;
   545→    
   546→    // Check WebSocket connection
   547→    if (!ws || ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
   548→        alert('WebSocket is not connected. Please wait a moment or refresh the page.');
   549→        return;
   550→    }
   551→    
   552→    try {
   553→        transcript.value = '';
   554→        enhancedTranscript.value = '';
   555→
   556→        // Check if stream is still valid, reinitialize ONLY if needed
   557→        let streamActive = false;
   558→        try {
   559→            streamActive = streamInitialized && stream && stream.active && 
   560→                          stream.getTracks().length > 0 && 
   561→                          stream.getTracks().every(track => track.readyState === 'live');
   562→        } catch (e) {
   563→            console.warn('Error checking stream status:', e);
   564→            streamActive = false;
   565→        }
   566→        
   567→        if (!streamActive) {
   568→            console.log('Reinitializing microphone stream...');
   569→            cleanupAudioResources();
   570→            
   571→            try {
   572→                stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ 
   573→                    audio: {
   574→                        channelCount: 1,
   575→                        echoCancellation: true,
   576→                        noiseSuppression: true,
   577→                        autoGainControl: true
   578→                    } 
   579→                });
   580→                streamInitialized = true;
   581→            } catch (err) {
   582→                console.error('getUserMedia error:', err);
   583→                throw new Error('Could not access microphone. Please check permissions.');
   584→            }
   585→        }
   586→
   587→        if (!stream) throw new Error('Failed to initialize audio stream');
   588→        
   589→        // Ensure AudioContext is active
   590→        if (!audioContext || audioContext.state === 'closed') {
   591→            await initAudio(stream);
   592→        } else if (audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
   593→            await audioContext.resume();
   594→        }
   595→
   596→        isRecording = true;
   597→        const modelSelect = document.getElementById('modelSelect');
   598→        const selectedModel = modelSelect ? modelSelect.value : 'gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15';
   599→        
   600→        // Create session in IndexedDB
   601→        if (storageAvailable) {
   602→            await createSession();
   603→        }
   604→        
   605→        const startMessage = { 
   606→            type: 'start_recording', 
   607→            model: selectedModel
   608→        };
   609→        console.log('Sending start_recording:', startMessage);
   610→        await ws.send(JSON.stringify(startMessage));
   611→        
   612→        startTimer();
   613→        recordButton.textContent = 'Stop';
   614→        recordButton.classList.add('recording');
   615→        if (replayButton) replayButton.disabled = true;
   616→        
   617→    } catch (error) {
   618→        console.error('Error starting recording:', error);
   619→        alert('Error accessing microphone: ' + error.message);
   620→    }
   621→}
   622→
   623→async function stopRecording() {
   624→    if (!isRecording) return;
   625→    
   626→    // Set stopping flag first to allow final audio processing
   627→    isStopping = true;
   628→    isRecording = false;
   629→    const durationMs = performance.now() - sessionStartTime;
   630→    
   631→    // Stop local timer immediately on stop
   632→    stopTimer();
   633→    
   634→    // Wait a bit to allow any in-flight onaudioprocess callbacks to complete
   635→    // This ensures we capture the last bit of audio data
   636→    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
   637→    
   638→    // Send any remaining audio buffer
   639→    if (audioBuffer.length > 0 && ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   640→        const sendBuffer = audioBuffer.slice();
   641→        ws.send(sendBuffer.buffer);
   642→        
   643→        // Store final chunk
   644→        if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId && sessionStartTime) {
   645→            const deltaMs = performance.now() - sessionStartTime;
   646→            await appendChunk(currentSessionId, {
   647→                seq: chunkSeq++,
   648→                deltaMs: deltaMs,
   649→                kind: 'audio',
   650→                payload: sendBuffer.buffer,
   651→                byteLength: sendBuffer.byteLength
   652→            });
   653→        }
   654→        
   655→        audioBuffer = new Int16Array(0);
   656→    }
   657→    
   658→    // Clear stopping flag
   659→    isStopping = false;
   660→    
   661→    // Wait a bit more to ensure all audio is sent before stopping
   662→    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   663→    await ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'stop_recording' }));
   664→    
   665→    // Complete session in IndexedDB
   666→    if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId) {
   667→        await completeSession(currentSessionId, durationMs);
   668→        currentSessionId = null;
   669→        sessionStartTime = null;
   670→        chunkSeq = 0;
   671→    }
   672→    
   673→    recordButton.textContent = 'Start';
   674→    recordButton.classList.remove('recording');
   675→    updateReplayButtonState();
   676→}
   677→
   678→// Replay functionality
   679→async function replayLastRecording() {
   680→    if (isRecording || isReplaying || !storageAvailable) return;
   681→    
   682→    const session = await getLatestCompletedSession();
   683→    if (!session) {
   684→        alert('No completed recording found to replay.');
   685→        return;
   686→    }
   687→    
   688→    if (isRecording) {
   689→        alert('Please stop recording before replaying.');
   690→        return;
   691→    }
   692→    
   693→    isReplaying = true;
   694→    recordButton.disabled = true;
   695→    if (replayButton) {
   696→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   697→        replayButton.title = 'Replaying...';
   698→        replayButton.style.animation = 'spin 1s linear infinite';
   699→    }
   700→    
   701→    try {
   702→        // Get chunks for this session
   703→        const chunks = await getSessionChunks(session.id);
   704→        if (chunks.length === 0) {
   705→            throw new Error('No chunks found for session');
   706→        }
   707→        
   708→        // Clear transcript
   709→        transcript.value = '';
   710→        enhancedTranscript.value = '';
   711→        
   712→        // Ensure WebSocket is connected
   713→        if (!wsConnected || ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
   714→            await new Promise((resolve) => {
   715→                const checkConnection = setInterval(() => {
   716→                    if (wsConnected && ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   717→                        clearInterval(checkConnection);
   718→                        resolve();
   719→                    }
   720→                }, 100);
   721→            });
   722→        }
   723→        
   724→        // Send start_recording message
   725→        const modelSelect = document.getElementById('modelSelect');
   726→        const selectedModel = modelSelect ? modelSelect.value : 'gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15';
   727→        
   728→        const startMessage = { 
   729→            type: 'start_recording', 
   730→            model: selectedModel
   731→        };
   732→        console.log('Sending start_recording:', startMessage);
   733→        await ws.send(JSON.stringify(startMessage));
   734→        
   735→        // Wait a bit for backend to initialize
   736→        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200));
   737→        
   738→        // Replay audio chunks - send as fast as possible
   739→        const audioChunks = chunks.filter(c => c.kind === 'audio' && c.payload);
   740→        
   741→        // Send all audio chunks immediately
   742→        for (const chunk of audioChunks) {
   743→            if (ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   744→                ws.send(chunk.payload);
   745→            } else {
   746→                throw new Error('WebSocket closed during replay');
   747→            }
   748→        }
   749→        
   750→        // Send stop_recording after all audio chunks
   751→        await ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'stop_recording' }));
   752→        
   753→    } catch (error) {
   754→        console.error('Error replaying recording:', error);
   755→        alert('Error replaying recording: ' + error.message);
   756→    } finally {
   757→        isReplaying = false;
   758→        recordButton.disabled = false;
   759→        updateReplayButtonState();
   760→    }
   761→}
   762→
   763→function updateReplayButtonState() {
   764→    if (!replayButton) return;
   765→    
   766→    if (!storageAvailable) {
   767→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   768→        replayButton.title = 'Local storage not available';
   769→        return;
   770→    }
   771→    
   772→    if (isRecording || isReplaying) {
   773→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   774→        if (isReplaying) {
   775→            replayButton.title = 'Replaying...';
   776→            replayButton.style.animation = 'spin 1s linear infinite';
   777→        } else {
   778→            replayButton.title = 'Recording in progress';
   779→            replayButton.style.animation = '';
   780→        }
   781→        return;
   782→    }
   783→    
   784→    // Check if there's a completed session
   785→    getLatestCompletedSession().then(session => {
   786→        if (session) {
   787→            replayButton.disabled = false;
   788→            replayButton.title = 'Replay last recording';
   789→            replayButton.style.animation = '';
   790→        } else {
   791→            replayButton.disabled = true;
   792→            replayButton.title = 'No recording to replay';
   793→            replayButton.style.animation = '';
   794→        }
   795→    });
   796→}
   797→
   798→// Event listeners
   799→recordButton.onclick = () => isRecording ? stopRecording() : startRecording();

import pytest
from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
from realtime_server import app, ReadabilityRequest, CorrectnessRequest, AskAIRequest
import json
from unittest.mock import patch, AsyncMock, MagicMock

client = TestClient(app)

@pytest.fixture
def mock_llm_processor():
    with patch('realtime_server.llm_processor') as mock:
        # Setup for sync processing
        mock.process_text_sync.return_value = "Mocked response"
        
        # Setup for async processing
        async def text_generator():
            yield "Mocked"
            yield " streaming"
            yield " response"
        mock.process_text.return_value = text_generator()
        
        yield mock

def test_enhance_readability(mock_llm_processor):
    request = ReadabilityRequest(text="Test text")
    response = client.post("/api/v1/readability", json=request.model_dump())
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert "Mocked streaming response" in response.text

def test_check_correctness(mock_llm_processor):
    request = CorrectnessRequest(text="Test fact checking")
    response = client.post("/api/v1/correctness", json=request.model_dump())
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert "Mocked streaming response" in response.text

@pytest.mark.skip(reason="ask_ai endpoint is temporarily disabled")
def test_ask_ai(mock_llm_processor):
    request = AskAIRequest(text="What is the meaning of life?")
    response = client.post("/api/v1/ask_ai", json=request.model_dump())
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert response.json()["answer"] == "Mocked response"

@pytest.mark.asyncio
async def test_websocket_endpoint():
    with patch('realtime_server.OpenAIRealtimeAudioTextClient') as mock_client:
        mock_instance = AsyncMock()
        mock_client.return_value = mock_instance
        mock_instance.connect = AsyncMock()
        mock_instance.close = AsyncMock()
        mock_instance.process_audio = AsyncMock(return_value={"text": "test"})

        with client.websocket_connect("/api/v1/ws") as websocket:
            # Send a test message
            data = {
                "audio": "base64_encoded_audio_data",
                "timestamp": "2024-01-01T00:00:00"
            }
            websocket.send_json(data)
            
            # Verify we get a response
            response = websocket.receive_json()
            assert "type" in response

def test_get_realtime_page():
    response = client.get("/")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert "text/html" in response.headers["content-type"]


def test_health_check():
    response = client.get("/health")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert response.json() == {"status": "ok"}


def test_get_old_redirects_to_root():
    response = client.get("/old", follow_redirects=False)
    assert response.status_code == 302
    assert response.headers["location"] == "/"


def test_get_main_js():
    response = client.get("/static/main.js")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert "application/javascript" in response.headers.get("content-type", "")
    assert "Cache-Control" in response.headers

"""Tests for config module."""
import config


def test_openai_realtime_model_is_string():
    assert isinstance(config.OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL, str)
    assert len(config.OPENAI_REALTIME_MODEL) > 0

            return_value=MagicMock(text="Test response")

class TestGeminiProcessor:
    def test_init_no_api_key(self):
        with patch.dict(os.environ, clear=True):
            with pytest.raises(EnvironmentError, match="GOOGLE_API_KEY is not set"):
                GeminiProcessor()

    def test_init_success(self, mock_env_vars, mock_genai):
        processor = GeminiProcessor()
        assert processor.default_model == 'gemini-1.5-pro'
        mock_genai.configure.assert_called_once_with(api_key='test_google_key')

    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_process_text(self, mock_env_vars, mock_genai):
        mock_model = mock_genai.GenerativeModel.return_value
        async def async_gen():
            for chunk in [MagicMock(text="Hello"), MagicMock(text=" World")]:
                yield chunk
        mock_model.generate_content_async.return_value = async_gen()

        processor = GeminiProcessor()
        result = []
        async for chunk in processor.process_text("input", "prompt"):
            result.append(chunk)
        assert result == ["Hello", " World"]
        mock_genai.GenerativeModel.return_value.generate_content_async.assert_called_once()

    def test_process_text_sync(self, mock_env_vars, mock_genai):
        processor = GeminiProcessor()
        result = processor.process_text_sync("input", "prompt")
        assert result == "Test response"
        mock_genai.GenerativeModel.return_value.generate_content.assert_called_once()

---

## COMPREHENSIVE BRAINWAVE SYSTEM OVERVIEW

I've thoroughly explored the Brainwave codebase. Here's a complete technical breakdown:

---

### 1. OVERALL ARCHITECTURE

**Framework & Technology Stack:**
- **Backend:** FastAPI with Uvicorn (Python 3.8+)
- **WebSocket Protocol:** Native WebSocket for real-time bidirectional communication
- **Frontend:** Vanilla JavaScript with Web Audio API, IndexedDB, and CSS3
- **AI Models:** OpenAI Realtime API integration (gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15 and gpt-realtime-1.5)
- **Audio Processing:** 48kHz to 24kHz resampling using SciPy
- **Storage:** IndexedDB for client-side replay capability
- **Testing:** pytest with async support (pytest-asyncio, pytest-mock)

**Key Files Structure:**
```
/home/gem/project/
├── realtime_server.py          # Main FastAPI server
├── openai_realtime_client.py   # OpenAI WebSocket client
├── realtime_client_base.py     # Abstract base class for providers
├── llm_processor.py            # LLM abstraction (GPT/Gemini)
├── prompts.py                  # Prompt templates
├── config.py                   # Configuration management
├── static/
│   ├── realtime.html          # HTML UI
│   ├── main.js                # Frontend logic (~950 lines)
│   └── style.css              # Styling with dark mode
├── tests/                      # Unit tests
└── requirements.txt            # Dependencies
```

---

### 2. WEBSOCKET/REALTIME API INTEGRATION

**Flow Architecture:**

```
Browser Client
    ↓ (WebSocket: /api/v1/ws)
FastAPI Server (realtime_server.py)
    ↓ (WebSocket)
OpenAI Realtime API
    ↓ (WebSocket: wss://api.openai.com/v1/realtime)
OpenAI Service
```

**Backend WebSocket Handler (`realtime_server.py:116-515`):**

1. **Connection Initialization:**
   - Accepts WebSocket at `/api/v1/ws`
   - Sends initial `status: "idle"` to frontend
   - Manages AudioProcessor for resampling (48kHz → 24kHz)

2. **Message Types:**
   - **Binary data:** Audio chunks from frontend
   - **Text messages:**
     - `start_recording`: Initializes OpenAI client with selected model
     - `stop_recording`: Commits audio, starts response generation

3. **OpenAI Integration (`openai_realtime_client.py:16-171`):**
   - Maintains WebSocket connection to OpenAI API
   - Handles base64-encoded audio transmission via `input_audio_buffer.append`
   - Registers handlers for various message types:
     - `response.text.delta`: Streams text output
     - `response.output_text.delta`: GA version of delta
     - `response.done`: Marks response completion
     - `session.updated`: Session configuration confirmation
   - Methods:
     - `connect()`: Establishes connection, configures session
     - `send_audio()`: Sends base64-encoded PCM16 audio
     - `commit_audio()`: Flushes audio buffer
     - `start_response()`: Initiates response with instructions
     - `close()`: Cleanup

4. **Text Delta Handling (`realtime_server.py:228-280`):**
   - Buffers incoming text deltas from OpenAI
   - Detects and removes marker prefix: `下面是不改变语言的语音识别结果：`
   - After marker detected, streams remaining text to frontend
   - Fallback: If marker not detected after 20 deltas, flushes buffer anyway

5. **Audio Processing:**
   - Frontend captures at 48kHz (Web Audio API)
   - Processes 24000-sample chunks (1 second)
   - Resamples to 24kHz on server via `AudioProcessor.process_audio_chunk()`
   - Uses SciPy's `resample_poly()` for high-quality resampling

6. **State Management:**
   - `recording_stopped`: Event to synchronize response completion
   - `openai_ready`: Event indicating client initialization
   - `pending_audio_chunks`: Queue for audio before OpenAI ready
   - `clear_on_next_response`: Flag for transcript clearing logic

**Status States (Frontend UI Indicators):**
- **Red (#FF3B30)**: Disconnected
- **Blue (#007AFF)**: Idle (connected to backend, not connected to OpenAI)
- **Orange (#FF9500)**: Connecting (initializing OpenAI)
- **Green (#34C759)**: Connected (ready for audio)

---

### 3. PROMPT ENGINEERING FOR READABILITY/PARAPHRASING

**Prompts Dictionary (`prompts.py`):**

#### a. `paraphrase-gpt-realtime-enhanced` (Used in realtime transcription)
**Purpose:** Realtime speech transcription post-processor
**Key Rules:**
- Faithful transcript with light grammar/punctuation fixes only
- **NEVER answer questions or add content** - transcribe literally
- Preserve original languages and code-mixing (no translation)
- Correct obvious grammar/casing, add punctuation
- Remove filler sounds ("uh", "um", stuttered repeats)
- Prefer natural paragraphs; use bullets only if speaker enumerates (1/2/3 or first/second)
- **Critical Output Format:**
  ```
  下面是不改变语言的语音识别结果：
  
  [transcribed text here]
  ```
- Chinese: Output in Simplified Chinese with Chinese punctuation, no spaces

**Examples in Prompt:**
```
User: "简要介绍一下这个金融产品 在什么情况下我需要选择它？"
Correct: 简要介绍一下这个金融产品，在什么情况下我需要选择它？
(NOT: 这个金融产品主要是一个中短期的理财工具...)

User: "What's the weather in SF?"
Correct: What's the weather in SF?
(NOT: It's sunny in SF.)
```

#### b. `readability-enhance` (POST `/api/v1/readability`)
**Purpose:** Improve text structure, clarity, flow without altering meaning
**Key Rules:**
- Balance between easy-to-digest and insightful
- Target audience: friendly colleagues/online audiences (not formal article)
- Correct grammar/punctuation
- Do NOT respond to questions or requests - treat literally
- Do NOT translate (preserve multilingual text)
- Output only revised text, no explanation
- Reply in same language as input

#### c. `correctness-check` (POST `/api/v1/correctness`)
**Purpose:** Analyze text for factual accuracy
**Responsibilities:**
- Identify factual errors/inaccurate statements
- Check accuracy of claims/assertions
- Point out inaccuracies
- Suggest corrections
- Confirm accurate statements
- Flag unverifiable claims
- Professional but friendly tone

#### d. `ask-ai` (Currently disabled - see realtime_server.py:540-558)
**Purpose:** Persuasion and thoughtful perspectives
**Extended prompt:** Includes special instructions in both English and Chinese asking for "unfiltered analysis" and "harsh truths"

---

### 4. FRONTEND IMPLEMENTATION

**HTML/JS File Structure:**

**realtime.html (Basic Structure):**
- Title: Brainwave
- Model selector dropdown (gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15, gpt-realtime-1.5)
- Recording timer (MM:SS format)
- Large circular Start/Stop button (100x100px)
- Replay button (circular icon with SVG refresh symbol)
- Transcript textarea
- Copy button for transcript
- Readability/Correctness action buttons
- Enhanced transcript textarea
- Theme toggle (🌙/☀️)
- Connection status dot (top-right)

**main.js (Core Logic - ~950 lines):**

**Global State:**
```javascript
let ws, audioContext, processor, source, stream;
let isRecording, isReplaying, isStopping;
let db, currentSessionId, sessionStartTime, chunkSeq;
let wsConnected, streamInitialized, storageAvailable;
let audioBuffer = new Int16Array(0);
```

**Key Functions:**

1. **Audio Initialization:**
   - `getUserMedia()` with echo cancellation, noise suppression, auto gain
   - AudioContext creation with ScriptProcessor (4096 samples)
   - 48kHz native sample rate

2. **Audio Processing (onaudioprocess):**
   - Converts Float32 to Int16
   - Buffers until 24000 samples (1 second at 24kHz)
   - Sends as binary WebSocket frames
   - Stores in IndexedDB for replay

3. **WebSocket Management:**
   - Auto-reconnect after 1 second if disconnected
   - Status-based UI updates
   - Message handling:
     - `status`: Connection state updates
     - `text`: Transcript streaming
     - `error`: Error alerts

4. **Recording Control:**
   - `startRecording()`: Initializes stream, sends `start_recording` message
   - `stopRecording()`: 
     - Sets `isStopping` flag to allow final audio processing
     - Waits 100ms for in-flight callbacks
     - Sends remaining audio buffer
     - Sends `stop_recording` message
     - Completes IndexedDB session

5. **IndexedDB Replay Feature:**
   - **Database:** `brainwave-replay` (v1)
   - **Object Stores:**
     - `sessions`: {id, createdAt, status, sampleRate, channelCount, durationMs}
     - `chunks`: {id, sessionId, seq, deltaMs, kind, payload, byteLength}
   
   - **Session Lifecycle:**
     - Create on startRecording
     - Append chunks during recording
     - Complete on stopRecording
     - Query for latest completed session
   
   - **Replay Workflow (`replayLastRecording()`):**
     - Retrieves latest completed session
     - Sends new `start_recording` message
     - Sends all audio chunks sequentially
     - Sends `stop_recording` message
     - Handles WebSocket reconnection during replay

6. **Text Enhancement Handlers:**
   - **Readability:** `POST /api/v1/readability` → Streams response
   - **Correctness:** `POST /api/v1/correctness` → Streams response
   - **Ask AI:** `POST /api/v1/ask_ai` → JSON response (currently disabled)
   - All use streaming with TextDecoder for progressive rendering

7. **Theme Management:**
   - `toggleTheme()`: Switches dark mode
   - Saves preference to localStorage
   - Dark theme class applied to `<body>`

**CSS Styling (style.css):**
- Clean Apple-inspired design
- Dark mode support with color variables
- Responsive (max-width: 480px media query)
- Animations: pulse (recording button), blink (connecting), spin (replay)
- Copy buttons with feedback animations

  - Supported: `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15`, `gpt-realtime-1.5`

- `GOOGLE_API_KEY`: Gemini API key (for alternative LLM processing)

- Environment variables override defaults

- .gitignore includes `.env`
- Never commit API keys

---

### 8. LLM PROCESSOR ABSTRACTION

**llm_processor.py:**
- Abstract base class `LLMProcessor`
- Two implementations:
  - `GeminiProcessor`: Uses google-generativeai
  - `GPTProcessor`: Uses OpenAI async/sync clients
- `get_llm_processor(model)`: Factory that selects based on model prefix
  - `gemini*` → GeminiProcessor
  - `gpt-*` or `o1-*` → GPTProcessor

**API Endpoints Using LLM:**
1. `POST /api/v1/readability` → GPT-4o streaming
2. `POST /api/v1/correctness` → GPT-4o-search-preview streaming
3. `POST /api/v1/ask_ai` → DISABLED (was using O1-mini)

**Test Files:**
- `test_config.py`: Configuration validation
- `test_llm_processor.py`: LLM processor mocking with Gemini/GPT
- `test_realtime_server.py`: FastAPI endpoints, WebSocket, readability/correctness
- `test_openai_realtime_client.py`: OpenAI client integration
- `test_audio_processor.py`: Audio resampling verification

**Test Setup:**
```bash

```

**Mocking Strategy:**
- Uses `unittest.mock` for API clients
- Avoids real API calls in test environment
- Mock environment variables: `OPENAI_API_KEY='test_key'`

---

### 10. DATA FLOW DIAGRAM

```
User speaks
    ↓
Web Audio API (48kHz)
    ↓
ScriptProcessor buffers
    ↓
24000 samples (1 sec)
    ↓
WebSocket binary frame
    ↓
realtime_server.py (receives)
    ↓
AudioProcessor.process_audio_chunk()
    ↓
SciPy resample_poly (48kHz → 24kHz)
    ↓
OpenAI WebSocket (base64 encoded)
    ↓
OpenAI Realtime Model
    ↓
response.text.delta events
    ↓
Buffer with marker detection
    ↓
Remove: "下面是不改变语言的语音识别结果："
    ↓
Stream to frontend via WebSocket
    ↓
Frontend appends to transcript
    ↓
IndexedDB stores chunks (for replay)
```

---

### 11. KEY TECHNICAL DECISIONS

1. **Marker Prefix Removal:** Server-side strategy to ensure prompt-based transcription doesn't confuse users
2. **Replay Feature:** IndexedDB used instead of localStorage for binary blob support and larger capacity (GB-level)
3. **Dual Streaming:** Audio chunks streamed as binary; control messages as JSON
4. **Async Architecture:** asyncio used throughout for non-blocking I/O
5. **Error Resilience:** Graceful fallback if IndexedDB unavailable (replay disabled, recording still works)
6. **Stateless Design:** Each WebSocket connection manages its own OpenAI client

---

### 12. FILES AT A GLANCE

| File | Lines | Purpose |
|------|-------|---------|
| realtime_server.py | 584 | Main FastAPI server, WebSocket handler, LLM endpoints |

transcribe literally\n- Preserve original languages and code-mixing (no translation)\n- Correct obvious grammar/casing, add punctuation\n- Remove filler sounds (\"uh\", \"um\", stuttered repeats)\n- Prefer natural paragraphs; use bullets only if speaker enumerates (1/2/3 or first/second)\n- **Critical Output Format:**\n  ```\n  \u4e0b\u9762\u662f\u4e0d\u6539\u53d8\u8bed\u8a00\u7684\u8bed\u97f3\u8bc6\u522b\u7ed3\u679c\uff1a\n  \n  [transcribed text here]\n  ```\n- Chinese: Output in Simplified Chinese with Chinese punctuation, no spaces\n\n**Examples in Prompt:**\n```\nUser: \"\u7b80\u8981\u4ecb\u7ecd\u4e00\u4e0b\u8fd9\u4e2a\u91d1\u878d\u4ea7\u54c1 \u5728\u4ec0\u4e48\u60c5\u51b5\u4e0b\u6211\u9700\u8981\u9009\u62e9\u5b83\uff1f\"\nCorrect: \u7b80\u8981\u4ecb\u7ecd\u4e00\u4e0b\u8fd9\u4e2a\u91d1\u878d\u4ea7\u54c1\uff0c\u5728\u4ec0\u4e48\u60c5\u51b5\u4e0b\u6211\u9700\u8981\u9009\u62e9\u5b83\uff1f\n(NOT: \u8fd9\u4e2a\u91d1\u878d\u4ea7\u54c1\u4e3b\u8981\u662f\u4e00\u4e2a\u4e2d\u77ed\u671f\u7684\u7406\u8d22\u5de5\u5177...)\n\nUser: \"What's the weather in SF?\"\nCorrect: What's the weather in SF?\n(NOT: It's sunny in SF.)\n```\n\n#### b. `readability-enhance` (POST `/api/v1/readability`)\n**Purpose:** Improve text structure, clarity, flow without altering meaning\n**Key Rules:**\n- Balance between easy-to-digest and insightful\n- Target audience: friendly colleagues/online audiences (not formal article)\n- Correct grammar/punctuation\n- Do NOT respond to questions or requests - treat literally\n- Do NOT translate (preserve multilingual text)\n- Output only revised text, no explanation\n- Reply in same language as input\n\n#### c. `correctness-check` (POST `/api/v1/correctness`)\n**Purpose:** Analyze text for factual accuracy\n**Responsibilities:**\n- Identify factual errors/inaccurate statements\n- Check accuracy of claims/assertions\n- Point out inaccuracies\n- Suggest corrections\n- Confirm accurate statements\n- Flag unverifiable claims\n- Professional but friendly tone\n\n#### d. `ask-ai` (Currently disabled - Query for latest completed session\n   \n   - **Replay Workflow (`replayLastRecording()`):**\n     - Retrieves latest completed session\n     - Sends new `start_recording` message\n     - Sends all audio chunks sequentially\n     - Sends `stop_recording` message\n     - Handles WebSocket reconnection during replay\n\n6. **Text Enhancement Handlers:**\n   - **Readability:** `POST /api/v1/readability` \u2192 Streams response\n   - KEY TECHNICAL DECISIONS\n\n1. **Marker Prefix Removal:** Server-side strategy to ensure prompt-based transcription doesn't confuse users\n2. **Replay Feature:** IndexedDB used instead of localStorage for binary blob support and larger capacity (GB-level)\n3. **Dual Streaming:** Audio chunks streamed as binary; control messages as JSON\n4. **Async Architecture:** asyncio used throughout for non-blocking I/O\n5. **Error Resilience:** Graceful fallback if IndexedDB unavailable (replay disabled, recording still works)\n6. **Stateless Design:** Each WebSocket connection manages its own OpenAI client\n\n---\n\n### 12. 'use strict';

/* ===== DOM refs ===== */
const quickBtn      = document.getElementById('quick-btn');
const quickRing     = document.getElementById('quick-ring');

const brainstormRing = document.getElementById('brainstorm-ring');
const micHint       = document.getElementById('mic-hint');
const liveTranscript = document.getElementById('live-transcript');
const liveText      = document.getElementById('live-text');
const transcriptBar = document.getElementById('transcript-bar');
const transcriptText = document.getElementById('transcript-text');
const sendBtn       = document.getElementById('send-btn');
const discardBtn    = document.getElementById('discard-btn');
const transcriptCleanedLabel = document.getElementById('transcript-cleaned-label');
const transcriptRawWrap = document.getElementById('transcript-raw-wrap');
const transcriptRawText = document.getElementById('transcript-raw-text');
const messagesEl    = document.getElementById('messages');
const messagesEmpty = document.getElementById('messages-empty');
const notSupported  = document.getElementById('not-supported');
const settingsBtn   = document.getElementById('settings-btn');
const modalOverlay  = document.getElementById('modal-overlay');
const modalClose    = document.getElementById('modal-close');
const webhookInput  = document.getElementById('webhook-url');
const langSelect    = document.getElementById('lang-select');
const saveSettings  = document.getElementById('save-settings');
const summarizeInput = document.getElementById('summarize-url');
const wakeBtn       = document.getElementById('wake-btn');

/* ===== State ===== */
let recognition     = null;
let isListening     = false;
let activeMode      = null; // 'quick' | 'brainstorm' | null
let finalTranscript = '';
let interimText     = '';
let silenceTimer    = null;
const SILENCE_DELAY = 3500; // ms — only used in quick mode

/* ===== Brainstorm summary state ===== */
let _pendingSummary = null; // Promise resolving to summarized text, or null

/* ===== Transcript cleaning ===== */
function cleanTranscript(raw) {
  if (!raw) return raw;

  // Strip obvious spoken filler sounds
  let text = raw.replace(/\b(um+|uh+|er+|hmm+|mhm)\b\s*/gi, ' ');

  // Collapse multiple whitespace
  text = text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();

  // Capitalize first letter
  if (text) {
    text = text.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + text.slice(1);
  }

  // Capitalize first letter after sentence-ending punctuation
  text = text.replace(/([.!?])\s+([a-z])/g, (_, p, l) => `${p} ${l.toUpperCase()}`);

  // Add terminal period if absent
  if (text && !/[.!?…]$/.test(text)) {
    text += '.';
  }

  return text;
}

/* ===== Brainstorm post-processing ===== */
async function summarizeBrainstorm(rawText) {
  const endpoint = localStorage.getItem('summarizeUrl') || '';
  if (!endpoint) return cleanTranscript(rawText);

  try {
    const res = await fetch(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ text: rawText }),
    });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
    const data = await res.json();
    const summary = (data.summary || data.text || '').trim();
    return summary || cleanTranscript(rawText);
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn('Summarize error:', err);
    return cleanTranscript(rawText);
  }
}

/* ===== Brainstorm continuity ===== */
// Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically; we restart seamlessly in brainstorm mode
// and preserve accumulated transcript across restarts.
let brainstormAccumulator  = '';
let _brainstormRestarting  = false;

/* ===== Wake word state ===== */
let wakeRecognition       = null;
let wakeMode              = false;
let wakeTriggered         = false; // transitioning from wake → main recording
let wakeTriggeredRecording = false; // current recording was initiated by wake word
let wakeRestartTimer      = null;
const WAKE_PHRASES        = ['hey chill', 'hey chil']; // core phrase + common partial

/* ===== Audio Feedback ===== */
let audioCtx = null;

function getAudioContext() {
  if (!audioCtx) {
    audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
  }
  if (audioCtx.state === 'suspended') {
    audioCtx.resume();
  }
  return audioCtx;
}

// Prime the AudioContext on first user interaction so it's ready for hands-free sends
function primeAudio() {
  try { getAudioContext(); } catch (_) {}
}

function _playTone(ctx, frequency, startTime, duration, gain) {
  const osc  = ctx.createOscillator();
  const amp  = ctx.createGain();
  osc.connect(amp);
  amp.connect(ctx.destination);
  osc.type = 'sine';
  osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(frequency, startTime);
  amp.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startTime);
  amp.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(gain, startTime + 0.01);
  amp.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, startTime + duration);
  osc.start(startTime);
  osc.stop(startTime + duration);
}

function playSuccessSound() {
  // Prefer speech synthesis — "Got it" is immediately understood
  if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
    const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance('Got it');
    utt.rate   = 1.1;
    utt.pitch  = 1.1;
    utt.volume = 1;
    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    return;
  }
  // Fallback: ascending double chime
  try {
    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    _playTone(ctx, 880,  now,        0.22, 0.30); // A5
    _playTone(ctx, 1320, now + 0.18, 0.38, 0.25); // E6
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
  }
}

function playFailureSound() {
  // Descending dissonant triple-tone — distinct "uh-oh" signal
  try {
    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    _playTone(ctx, 330, now,        0.18, 0.40); // E4
    _playTone(ctx, 262, now + 0.15, 0.18, 0.40); // C4
    _playTone(ctx, 196, now + 0.30, 0.45, 0.35); // G3
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
  }
}

/* ===== Service Worker ===== */
if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
  navigator.serviceWorker.register('sw.js').catch(() => {/* silent */});
}

/* ===== Language preference ===== */
function getRecognitionLang() {
  return localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || navigator.language || 'en-US';
}

/* ===== Speech Recognition setup ===== */
const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;

if (!SpeechRecognition) {
  notSupported.hidden = false;
  quickBtn.disabled = true;
  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
  brainstormBtn.disabled = true;
  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
} else {
  initRecognition();
}

function initRecognition() {
  recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
  recognition.continuous     = true;
  recognition.interimResults = true;
  recognition.lang           = getRecognitionLang();
  recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;

  recognition.onstart = () => {
    if (_brainstormRestarting) {
      // Seamless brainstorm restart — preserve accumulated transcript, don't reset UI
      isListening = true;
      finalTranscript = brainstormAccumulator;
      interimText = '';
      _brainstormRestarting = false;
      return;
    }
    isListening = true;
    finalTranscript = '';
    brainstormAccumulator = '';
    interimText = '';
    setRecordingUI(true, activeMode);
  };

  recognition.onresult = (event) => {
    let interim = '';
    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
      const result = event.results[i];
      if (result.isFinal) {
        finalTranscript += result[0].transcript + ' ';
      } else {
        interim += result[0].transcript;
      }
    }
    interimText = interim;
    const displayText = (finalTranscript + interim).trim();
    updateLiveText(displayText);

    // Silence timer only applies to quick mode
    if (activeMode === 'quick') {
      resetSilenceTimer();
    }
  };

  recognition.onerror = (event) => {
    // 'no-speech' is common and expected — just stop cleanly
    if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
      console.warn('Speech recognition error:', event.error);
    }
    _brainstormRestarting = false;
    stopListening();
  };

  recognition.onend = () => {
    if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
      // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart seamlessly
      brainstormAccumulator = finalTranscript;
      _brainstormRestarting = true;
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
          try {
            recognition.start();
          } catch (_) {
            _brainstormRestarting = false;
            brainstormAccumulator = '';
            isListening = false;
            finishRecording();
          }
        } else {
          _brainstormRestarting = false;
        }
      }, 150);
      return;
    }
    // onend fires when recognition stops for any reason
    if (isListening) {
      // We didn't call stop manually yet; auto-stop happened
      finishRecording();
    }
  };
}

function resetSilenceTimer() {
  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
  silenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
    if (isListening) stopListening();
  }, SILENCE_DELAY);
}

/* ===== Recording controls ===== */
function startListening(mode) {
  if (!recognition || isListening) return;
  activeMode = mode;
  hideTranscriptBar();

  // Ensure wake recognition is stopped before starting main recording
  if (wakeMode) stopWakeRecognition();

  try {
    recognition.start();
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn('Could not start recognition:', e);
    // Re-init in case of invalid state
    initRecognition();
    try { recognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
  }

  if (mode === 'quick') {
    resetSilenceTimer();
  }
}

function stopListening() {
  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
  _brainstormRestarting = false; // prevent auto-restart in brainstorm
  isListening = false; // mark before calling stop so onend doesn't re-trigger finishRecording
  if (recognition) {
    try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
  }
  finishRecording();
}

function finishRecording() {
  const mode = activeMode;
  setRecordingUI(false, mode);
  const text = finalTranscript.trim();
  brainstormAccumulator = '';
  activeMode = null;
  if (text) {
    if (wakeTriggeredRecording) {
      // Hands-free path: auto-send without requiring a tap
      sendMessage(text);
    } else {
      showTranscriptBar(text, mode);
    }
  }
  wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
  // Resume passive wake word listening if mode is active
  if (wakeMode) scheduleWakeRestart();
  updateWakeHint();
}

/* ===== UI state helpers ===== */
function setRecordingUI(recording, mode) {
  const quickActive      = recording && mode === 'quick';
  const brainstormActive = recording && mode === 'brainstorm';

  // Quick button
  quickBtn.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);
  quickRing.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);
  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', quickActive ? 'true' : 'false');
  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', quickActive ? 'Stop recording' : 'Quick Request – tap to speak');

  // Brainstorm button
  brainstormBtn.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);
  brainstormRing.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);
  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', brainstormActive ? 'true' : 'false');
  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', brainstormActive ? 'Stop brainstorm recording' : 'Brainstorm – tap for continuous recording');

  // Shared hint
  if (quickActive) {
    micHint.textContent = 'Listening… tap Quick to stop';
    micHint.classList.add('active');
    micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active');
  } else if (brainstormActive) {
    micHint.textContent = 'Recording… tap Brainstorm to stop';
    micHint.classList.add('active', 'brainstorm-active');
  } else {
    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');
    updateWakeHint();
  }

  liveTranscript.hidden = !recording;
  liveTranscript.classList.toggle('brainstorm-mode', recording && mode === 'brainstorm');
  if (!recording) {
    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
  }
}

function updateLiveText(text) {
  if (text) {
    liveText.textContent = text;
    liveText.classList.add('has-text');
    // Auto-scroll to bottom so latest speech is always visible in brainstorm
    if (activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
      liveTranscript.scrollTop = liveTranscript.scrollHeight;
    }
  } else {
    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
  }
}

function showTranscriptBar(text, mode) {
  if (mode === 'brainstorm') {
    transcriptRawText.textContent = text;
    transcriptCleanedLabel.hidden = false;
    transcriptRawWrap.hidden = false;

    const endpoint = localStorage.getItem('summarizeUrl') || '';
    if (endpoint) {
      // Async path: show processing state, await AI summary
      transcriptText.textContent = 'Processing…';
      transcriptText.classList.add('processing');
      sendBtn.disabled = true;

      _pendingSummary = summarizeBrainstorm(text).then(summary => {
        // Only update if the transcript bar is still showing this result
        if (!transcriptBar.hidden) {
          transcriptText.textContent = summary;
          transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');
          sendBtn.disabled = false;
        }
        _pendingSummary = null;
      });
    } else {
      // Sync path: local regex cleanup
      transcriptText.textContent = cleanTranscript(text);
      transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');
      _pendingSummary = null;
    }
  } else {
    transcriptText.textContent = text;
    transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');
    transcriptCleanedLabel.hidden = true;
    transcriptRawWrap.hidden = true;
    _pendingSummary = null;
  }
  transcriptBar.hidden = false;
}

function hideTranscriptBar() {
  transcriptBar.hidden = true;
  transcriptText.textContent = '';
  transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');
  transcriptRawText.textContent = '';
  transcriptCleanedLabel.hidden = true;
  transcriptRawWrap.hidden = true;
  sendBtn.disabled = false;
  _pendingSummary = null;
}

/* ===== Button click handlers ===== */
quickBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
  primeAudio();
  if (isListening && activeMode === 'quick') {
    stopListening();
  } else if (!isListening) {
    wakeTriggeredRecording = false; // manual tap — show transcript bar after
    startListening('quick');
  }
});

brainstormBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
  primeAudio();
  if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
    stopListening();
  } else if (!isListening) {
    wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
    startListening('brainstorm');
  }
});

/* ===== Send / Discard ===== */
sendBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
  primeAudio();
  const text = transcriptText.textContent.trim();
  if (!text) return;
  hideTranscriptBar();
  await sendMessage(text);
});

discardBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
  hideTranscriptBar();
});

/* ===== Webhook send ===== */
async function sendMessage(text) {
  const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
  const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();
  const payload    = { text, source: 'hey-chill', timestamp };

  // Add message to history immediately
  const msgEl = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');

  if (!webhookUrl) {
    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');
    return;
  }

  try {
    const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');
    playSuccessSound();
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn('Webhook error:', err);
    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');
    playFailureSound();
  }
}

/* ===== Message history ===== */
function addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {
  // Hide empty state
  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';

  const el = document.createElement('div');
  el.className = `message ${status}`;

  const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {
    hour: '2-digit',
    minute: '2-digit',
  });

  const statusLabel = {
    sending:    'Sending…',
    sent:       'Sent',
    error:      'Failed',
    'no-webhook': 'No webhook',
  };

  el.innerHTML = `
    <p class="message-text">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>
    <div class="message-meta">
      <span class="message-time">${timeStr}</span>
      <span class="message-status">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>
    </div>
  `;

  messagesEl.appendChild(el);
  el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });
  return el;
}

function updateMessageStatus(el, status) {
  el.className = `message ${status}`;
  const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');
  const labels = {
    sent:         'Sent',
    error:        'Failed',
    'no-webhook': 'No webhook set',
  };
  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;
}

function escapeHtml(str) {
  return str
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
}

/* ===== Settings modal ===== */
settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettings);
modalClose.addEventListener('click',  closeSettings);
modalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
  if (e.target === modalOverlay) closeSettings();
});

document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
  if (e.key === 'Escape') closeSettings();
});

saveSettings.addEventListener('click', () => {
  const url = webhookInput.value.trim();
  localStorage.setItem('webhookUrl', url);

  const summarizeUrl = summarizeInput.value.trim();
  if (summarizeUrl) {
    localStorage.setItem('summarizeUrl', summarizeUrl);
  } else {
    localStorage.removeItem('summarizeUrl');
  }

  const lang = langSelect.value;
  const prevLang = localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || '';
  if (lang !== prevLang) {
    if (lang) {
      localStorage.setItem('recognitionLang', lang);
    } else {
      localStorage.removeItem('recognitionLang');
    }
    // Re-init recognition so the new language takes effect immediately
    if (!isListening) {
      initRecognition();
      if (wakeMode) {
        stopWakeRecognition();
        wakeRecognition = null;
        scheduleWakeRestart();
      }
    }
  }

  closeSettings();
});

function openSettings() {
  webhookInput.value    = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
  summarizeInput.value  = localStorage.getItem('summarizeUrl') || '';
  langSelect.value      = localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || '';
  modalOverlay.hidden   = false;
  webhookInput.focus();
}

function closeSettings() {
  modalOverlay.hidden = true;
}

/* ===== Wake Word Detection ===== */

function isWakePhrase(transcript) {
  return WAKE_PHRASES.some(phrase => transcript.includes(phrase));
}

function initWakeRecognition() {
  wakeRecognition = new SpeechRecognition();
  wakeRecognition.continuous     = true;
  wakeRecognition.interimResults = true;
  wakeRecognition.lang           = getRecognitionLang();
  wakeRecognition.maxAlternatives = 1;

  wakeRecognition.onresult = (event) => {
    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
      const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript.toLowerCase().trim();
      if (isWakePhrase(transcript)) {
        handleWakeWordDetected();
        return;
      }
    }
  };

  wakeRecognition.onerror = (event) => {
    if (event.error === 'not-allowed' || event.error === 'service-not-allowed') {
      // Microphone access denied — silently disable wake mode
      disableWakeMode();
      return;
    }
    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
      scheduleWakeRestart();
    }
  };

  wakeRecognition.onend = () => {
    // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart unless we
    // deliberately stopped it to hand off to main recording.
    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
      scheduleWakeRestart();
    }
  };
}

function startWakeRecognition() {
  if (!wakeRecognition) initWakeRecognition();
  wakeTriggered = false;
  quickRing.classList.add('listening-passive'); // passive glow on quick button only
  try {
    wakeRecognition.start();
  } catch (e) {
    // InvalidStateError when already started — reinit and retry
    initWakeRecognition();
    try { wakeRecognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
  }
}

function stopWakeRecognition() {
  quickRing.classList.remove('listening-passive');
  if (wakeRecognition) {
    try { wakeRecognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
  }
}

function scheduleWakeRestart() {
  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
  wakeRestartTimer = setTimeout(() => {
    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
      startWakeRecognition();
    }
  }, 300);
}

function handleWakeWordDetected() {
  if (isListening || wakeTriggered) return;
  wakeTriggered = true;
  wakeTriggeredRecording = true; // flag so finishRecording auto-sends
  stopWakeRecognition();
  // Give the recognition engine a moment to fully stop before starting main recording
  setTimeout(() => {
    wakeTriggered = false;
    startListening('quick'); // wake word always triggers quick mode
  }, 250);
}

function enableWakeMode() {
  wakeMode = true;
  wakeBtn.classList.add('wake-active');
  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Disable wake word');
  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: ON';
  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '1');
  updateWakeHint();
  if (!isListening) startWakeRecognition();
}

function disableWakeMode() {
  wakeMode = false;
  wakeBtn.classList.remove('wake-active');
  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enable wake word');
  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: Hey Chill';
  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '0');
  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
  stopWakeRecognition();
  updateWakeHint();
}

function updateWakeHint() {
  if (!isListening) {
    micHint.textContent = wakeMode ? 'Say "Hey Chill" or tap Quick' : '';
    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');
  }
}

wakeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
  primeAudio();
  if (wakeMode) {
    disableWakeMode();
  } else {
    enableWakeMode();
  }
});

// Restore wake mode preference across sessions
if (SpeechRecognition && localStorage.getItem('wakeMode') === '1') {
  enableWakeMode();
}

'true' : 'false');\n  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', quickActive ? micHint.classList.add('active', 'brainstorm-active');\n  } else {\n    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');\n    updateWakeHint();\n  }\n\n  liveTranscript.hidden = !recording;\n  liveTranscript.classList.toggle('brainstorm-mode', recording && mode === 'brainstorm');\n  if (!recording) {\n    liveText.textContent = 'Listening\u2026';\n    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');\n  }\n}\n\nfunction updateLiveText(text) {\n  if (text) {\n    liveText.textContent = text;\n    liveText.classList.add('has-text');\n    // Auto-scroll to (!transcriptBar.hidden) {\n          transcriptText.textContent = summary;\n          transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');\n          sendBtn.disabled = false;\n        }\n        _pendingSummary = null;\n      });\n    } else {\n      // Sync path: local regex cleanup\n      transcriptText.textContent = cleanTranscript(text);\n      transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');\n      _pendingSummary = null;\n    }\n  } else {\n    transcriptText.textContent = text;\n    transcriptText.classList.remove('processing');\n ASSISTANTMESSAGE #65
Now I have a thorough understanding of both codebases. Let me write a comprehensive architecture proposal. **Hey Chill Summary:** - Vanilla JS PWA (no backend) - Uses Web Speech API (browser-native, free, limited compared to OpenAI) - Two modes: Quick (VAD auto-stop at 3.5s silence) and Brainstorm (continuous, manual stop) - After brainstorm: shows raw + "cleaned" text, offers webhook send or discard - Post-processing: currently just local regex (filler word removal, capitalization, period) OR a configurable HTTP endpoint for "summarize" - Webhook sends the text with source and timestamp to a configured URL, triggered by wake word "Hey Chill" - PWA with manifest and service worker, deployed statically on Vercel, supports en-US and zh-HK **Brainwave Summary:** - FastAPI backend with OpenAI Realtime API over WebSocket, handling 48kHz to 24kHz audio resampling for real-time transcription with paraphrasing, then post-processing through readability and correction endpoints - IndexedDB replay feature, model selection between gpt-realtime-mini and gpt-realtime-1.5, dark mode support, no Docker or deployment config needed Now I'm thinking through the architecture proposal. The fork strategy makes sense—I'd keep Brainwave's FastAPI backend, WebSocket handling, OpenAI Realtime client, audio resampling, and the readability/correctness post-processing, while bringing over Hey Chill's quick mode with Web Speech API, wake word detection, PWA setup, and UI patterns. The frontend would need to support both modes: quick mode using Web Speech API directly without backend, and brainstorm mode leveraging Brainwave's WebSocket infrastructure. For backend hosting, Vercel's serverless functions won't work since they can't maintain persistent WebSocket connections that the Realtime API needs. Railway or Fly.io are solid options with persistent containers, though self-hosting on the local machine would be free if reliability isn't a concern. For a personal use case, self-hosted Docker makes sense; for anything more production-oriented, I'd lean toward Railway or Fly.io. Now I'm thinking through the architecture itself. The two-mode approach is really clean—Quick mode stays lightweight using Web Speech API with a simple webhook, while Brainstorm mode taps into the full Brainwave backend with WebSocket and OpenAI Realtime for deeper processing. After the brainstorm transcript comes back, I need to decide on post-processing: either a readability enhancement using the existing Brainwave prompt, or a new inspire-or-correct endpoint that handles both inspiring new ideas and refining the user's thinking in one call. Actually, I think splitting this into two separate buttons makes more sense—one for Correctness (which already exists in Brainwave) and one for Inspire (which needs a new prompt focused on generating related ideas and challenging assumptions). For the LLM choices, Readability and Correctness both use GPT-4o with search capabilities already built in, while Inspire would be GPT-4o with a fresh prompt. On the cost side, I'm calculating the OpenAI Realtime pricing—it's $2.50 per million tokens for audio input and $10 per million for audio output, though since we're only outputting text, the actual cost should be lower than the full audio output rate. I need to estimate the text output costs too—transcription would generate a few hundred tokens, and running that through GPT-4o for polish is negligible. The exact pricing for the newer realtime models isn't entirely clear to me, so I'll work with rough estimates based on what I know. Now I'm mapping out the migration strategy: starting with forking Brainwave and setting up Docker, then adding the Quick mode with Web Speech API to the frontend, redesigning the UI to match Hey Chill's aesthetic, integrating the Inspire endpoint with its prompt, and finally deploying to migrate existing users over. Generating markdown proposal...
