Now I have everything I need. Let me write the architecture proposal. --- # Hey Chill × Brainwave — Architecture Proposal ## 1. Current State ### Hey Chill (chillkimtest-oss/hey-chill) | Aspect | Detail | |---|---| | Stack | Vanilla JS PWA — zero backend | | Deployment | Vercel static hosting | | Transcription | Browser Web Speech API (`webkitSpeechRecognition`) — free, but limited accuracy | | Quick mode | Push-to-talk with 3.5 s silence auto-stop → webhook POST | | Brainstorm mode | Continuous recording (manual stop) → local regex cleanup OR configurable `/summarize` endpoint | | Post-processing | Local: strip fillers, capitalize, add period. Remote: single configurable URL returning `{ summary }` | | Output | Sends cleaned text to a webhook URL (`{ text, source, timestamp }`) | | PWA features | `manifest.json`, service worker, installable | | Wake word | "Hey Chill" via Web Speech API | | Languages | `en-US`, `zh-HK` (Cantonese) | **Key gaps vs. Kim's requirements:** No Readability Enhancement, no Inspire/Correct step, no real-time transcription quality (Web Speech API accuracy is unreliable especially for mixed-language), no structured post-processing pipeline. --- ### Brainwave (this repo) | Aspect | Detail | |---|---| | Stack | FastAPI + Uvicorn (Python), vanilla JS frontend | | Transcription | OpenAI Realtime API via WebSocket — high accuracy, multilingual, code-switching | | Audio pipeline | 48 kHz → 24 kHz resampling (SciPy), PCM16 streaming | | Transcription prompt | Faithful transcript, filler removal, correct punctuation, marker prefix for detection | | Readability endpoint | `POST /api/v1/readability` → GPT-4o streaming | | Correctness endpoint | `POST /api/v1/correctness` → GPT-4o-search-preview streaming | | Replay | IndexedDB records all audio chunks; replay re-submits them | | Model selection | `gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15` (default) or `gpt-realtime-1.5` | | Deployment | Manual `uvicorn` — no Docker, no cloud config | **What Brainwave does well:** Real-time Realtime API proxying, sophisticated prompts, streaming UX, IndexedDB replay, LLM abstraction (GPT/Gemini). **What it lacks:** Quick mode, webhook integration, wake word, PWA shell, Hey Chill's polished two-button UX. --- ## 2. Brainwave Architecture — Deep Dive ``` Browser ──────── WS binary (PCM16) ──────► FastAPI /api/v1/ws │ ┌───────────────────┘ │ AudioProcessor │ 48kHz → 24kHz (SciPy) ▼ OpenAI Realtime API (WSS) gpt-realtime-mini / gpt-realtime-1.5 Mode: text-only output Prompt: paraphrase-gpt-realtime-enhanced │ response.text.delta events │ Buffer + strip marker prefix │ Stream text back to browser WS │ Browser appends to textarea │ User clicks Readability/Correctness │ POST /api/v1/readability POST /api/v1/correctness │ GPT-4o streaming │ Server-sent stream → browser ``` **Prompt design highlights:** - `paraphrase-gpt-realtime-enhanced`: Output must start with marker `下面是不改变语言的语音识别结果：`, then clean transcript. Server strips marker before streaming to user. Prevents model from answering questions or adding content. - `readability-enhance`: Improve flow/structure, preserve intent, do not translate, stream only revised text. - `correctness-check`: Identify factual errors, suggest corrections, flag unverifiable claims. --- ## 3. Recommended Architecture ### Decision: Fork Brainwave + Surgically Graft Hey Chill's Frontend **Do NOT migrate Hey Chill into Brainwave** in a big-bang rewrite. Instead, evolve Brainwave's frontend to be a superset of Hey Chill by adding Quick mode, webhook, wake word, and PWA capabilities alongside the existing Realtime API flow. ``` ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │ Hey Chill v2 (Forked Brainwave) │ │ │ │ ┌─────────────────┐ ┌──────────────────────────┐ │ │ │ Quick Mode │ │ Brainstorm Mode │ │ │ │ (Hey Chill UX) │ │ (Brainwave-powered) │ │ │ │ │ │ │ │ │ │ Web Speech API │ │ WebSocket ──► FastAPI │ │ │ │ (browser-native)│ │ OpenAI Realtime API │ │ │ │ 3.5s silence │ │ Streaming transcript │ │ │ │ → webhook POST │ │ │ │ │ │ NO backend req │ │ ┌────────────────────┐ │ │ │ └─────────────────┘ │ │ Post-Processing │ │ │ │ │ │ A. Readability │ │ │ │ Wake word: "Hey Chill" │ │ B. Inspire/Correct│ │ │ │ PWA manifest + SW │ └────────────────────┘ │ │ │ Message history │ → webhook POST (optional)│ │ │ Settings modal └──────────────────────────┘ │ └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │ WebSocket / HTTP ▼ ┌─────────────────────────┐ │ FastAPI Backend │ │ (Docker container) │ │ │ │ /api/v1/ws │ ──► OpenAI Realtime API │ /api/v1/readability │ ──► GPT-4o (streaming) │ /api/v1/correctness │ ──► GPT-4o search (streaming) │ /api/v1/inspire │ ──► GPT-4o (new endpoint) └─────────────────────────┘ ``` ### What to keep from Brainwave (unchanged) - `realtime_server.py` — all WebSocket and LLM endpoints - `openai_realtime_client.py` — OpenAI Realtime client - `realtime_client_base.py` — provider abstraction - `llm_processor.py` — GPT/Gemini abstraction - `config.py` — env var loading - `prompts.py` — paraphrase + readability + correctness prompts (add inspire) - `requirements.txt` — unchanged - `tests/` — all existing tests remain valid ### What to keep from Brainwave (modify) - `static/realtime.html` → evolve into Hey Chill's two-button layout with message history, settings modal, and the existing transcript/action area - `static/main.js` → significant additions (Quick mode, wake word, webhook, settings), preserve WebSocket/IndexedDB/replay core - `static/style.css` → add Hey Chill's design tokens, two-button layout, message history, modal styles ### What to bring in from Hey Chill | File | What to migrate | How | |---|---|---| | `app.js` | Quick mode logic, wake word detection, webhook send, message history, settings modal | Merge into `main.js` as separate sections | | `index.html` | Two-button layout, header, message history panel, transcript bar with raw/cleaned | Merge into `realtime.html` | | `style.css` | Mode button styles, quick-ring, brainstorm-ring, message history, modal | Merge into `style.css` | | `manifest.json` | PWA metadata, icons | Copy as-is, update `name` and `start_url` | | `sw.js` | Service worker caching | Copy as-is | | `icons/` | SVG icons | Copy as-is | ### New endpoint: `/api/v1/inspire` ```python # realtime_server.py — add alongside /readability and /correctness @app.post("/api/v1/inspire") async def inspire_endpoint(request: Request): body = await request.json() text = body.get("text", "") prompt = prompts["inspire-or-challenge"] # Stream GPT-4o response ... ``` ```python # prompts.py — new entry "inspire-or-challenge": """ You are a sharp thinking partner. The user has just spoken their thoughts. Your job is to either: 1. INSPIRE: Extend their thinking with related ideas, novel angles, or unexplored connections. 2. CHALLENGE: Respectfully push back on assumptions, point out blind spots, or reframe the problem. Choose whichever is more valuable given the context. - Be concrete, not generic. No platitudes. - Keep it conversational — like a smart colleague, not a lecturer. - Match the input language. Do NOT translate. - Output only your response. No meta-commentary. """ ``` ### Post-processing UI flow (Brainstorm mode) ``` [Recording stops] │ ▼ Streaming transcript appears in textarea │ ▼ Two action buttons appear: ┌──────────────────┐ ┌──────────────────────┐ │ ✨ Readability │ │ 💡 Inspire / Correct │ └──────────────────┘ └──────────────────────┘ │ │ POST /readability POST /inspire Stream into enhanced Stream into enhanced textarea below textarea below │ │ Optional: Webhook send button appears ``` --- ## 4. Backend Hosting ### Option Analysis | Option | Pros | Cons | Cost | |---|---|---|---| | **Vercel serverless** | Zero ops, auto-deploy from Git | No persistent WebSocket support — Vercel functions timeout at 10-300s, cannot proxy long-lived WSS connections | N/A — technically not viable | | **Railway** | One-click Python deploy, persistent containers, GitHub integration, custom domains | Cold starts on free tier, egress costs | ~$5–$10/month (Starter) | | **Fly.io** | Docker-native, persistent VMs, global edge, good free tier | Slightly more config than Railway, Docker required | Free for 1 shared-cpu VM, ~$3–$5/month for always-on | | **Self-hosted 192.168.101.151** | Zero cost, no cold starts, full control, already on Docker infrastructure | Requires public IP / reverse proxy / tunneling, home network reliability, no auto-scaling | $0 (infrastructure cost) | ### Recommendation **Phase 1 (personal/dev use): Self-hosted at 192.168.101.151** This repo has no Docker config yet, but adding it is 20 lines. With an existing Docker host and a reverse proxy (e.g., Caddy or nginx), this is: - Zero monthly cost - Fastest iteration cycle - No latency to cloud - Can use Cloudflare Tunnel (free) to avoid exposing home IP ```dockerfile # Dockerfile (add to repo root) FROM python:3.11-slim WORKDIR /app COPY requirements.txt . RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt COPY . . EXPOSE 3005 CMD ["uvicorn", "realtime_server:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "3005"] ``` **Phase 2 (if public traffic): Railway or Fly.io** Railway is simpler for Python (no Dockerfile required). Fly.io is better if Docker is already in the workflow. Neither supports static hosting well — keep static assets on Vercel (or serve from FastAPI's `StaticFiles` mount, which Brainwave already does). **Hybrid deployment (recommended for production):** ``` Vercel (static CDN) Railway / Fly.io / Self-hosted │ │ ├── index.html ├── FastAPI /api/v1/ws ├── app.js ├── /api/v1/readability ├── style.css ├── /api/v1/correctness ├── sw.js └── /api/v1/inspire └── manifest.json │ WebSocket / fetch to BACKEND_URL └────────────────────────────────► ``` The frontend config just needs `BACKEND_URL` set (currently hardcoded as relative path — needs one change to support cross-origin backend). --- ## 5. Migration Plan (Phased) ### Phase 0 — Setup (Day 1) - Fork Brainwave → new repo (e.g., `hey-chill-v2` or rename) - Add `Dockerfile` + `docker-compose.yml` - Deploy to self-hosted Docker host (192.168.101.151) - Verify existing Brainwave functionality works at new URL - Add `BACKEND_URL` config to frontend (replace relative `/api` with configurable base URL) **Deliverable:** Brainwave running on Docker, accessible at `https://chill.yourdomain.com/api` ### Phase 1 — Add Quick Mode (2–3 days) - Merge Hey Chill's `app.js` Quick mode section into `main.js` - `startListening('quick')` with Web Speech API - 3.5 s silence auto-stop - Webhook POST - Message history panel - Settings modal (webhook URL, language, summarize URL) - Update `realtime.html` with two-button layout - Update `style.css` with Hey Chill's mode-button design - **No backend changes needed for this phase** **Deliverable:** Both Quick mode (Web Speech) and Brainstorm mode (Realtime API) work. Quick mode needs zero backend. ### Phase 2 — Post-processing UX (2–3 days) - Update brainstorm stop flow: - Show raw transcript in textarea (as now) - Show two action buttons: "Readability" and "Inspire / Correct" - Remove the old single Correctness button - Add `/api/v1/inspire` endpoint + prompt to backend - Wire up streaming response into enhanced textarea - Add optional webhook send after enhancement - Add "Inspire" tab to existing enhanced textarea area **Deliverable:** Full post-processing pipeline working as Kim specified. ### Phase 3 — PWA + Polish (1–2 days) - Copy `manifest.json`, `sw.js`, `icons/` from Hey Chill - Add wake word ("Hey Chill" → triggers brainstorm recording) - Dark/light theme toggle (already in Brainwave CSS) - Mobile viewport polish - Update `sw.js` cache list for new file names **Deliverable:** Installable PWA, wake word, polished mobile UX. ### Phase 4 — DNS Cutover (1 day) - Point `heychill.yourdomain.com` to new deployment - Old Hey Chill Vercel deployment remains live during parallel period - Communicate to Kim for sign-off before switching DNS --- ## 6. Cost Estimates ### OpenAI Realtime API (per session) The Realtime API charges for audio input tokens. Audio tokens: **1 second ≈ 25 tokens** (PCM16 at 24 kHz, OpenAI's encoding). | Session length | Audio tokens | gpt-realtime-mini cost | gpt-realtime-1.5 cost | |---|---|---|---| | 2 min brainstorm | 3,000 | ~$0.008 | ~$0.036 | | 5 min brainstorm | 7,500 | ~$0.019 | ~$0.090 | | 10 min brainstorm | 15,000 | ~$0.038 | ~$0.180 | > Pricing basis: gpt-realtime-mini ~$2.50/1M audio input, ~$10/1M text output; gpt-realtime-1.5 ~$12/1M audio input. Text output (transcript tokens) is ~200–500 tokens for a 5-min session — negligible cost. ### Post-processing LLM (per session, GPT-4o) After brainstorm, user clicks one of two actions: | Call | Input tokens | Output tokens | GPT-4o cost | |---|---|---|---| | Readability (500-word transcript) | ~700 | ~700 | ~$0.007 | | Inspire/Correct (500-word transcript) | ~700 | ~500 | ~$0.006 | > GPT-4o pricing: $2.50/1M input, $10/1M output (as of early 2026 — verify at time of implementation). ### Total Per-Session Cost | Scenario | Realtime (mini) | Post-processing | Total | |---|---|---|---| | 2-min session + readability | $0.008 | $0.007 | **~$0.015** | | 5-min session + inspire | $0.019 | $0.006 | **~$0.025** | | 10-min session + both actions | $0.038 | $0.013 | **~$0.051** | **Monthly cost estimate** (assuming ~50 brainstorm sessions/month, 5 min average): - ~50 × $0.025 = **~$1.25/month** in API costs for personal use - Quick mode (Web Speech API): **$0** — free, browser-native **Note:** gpt-realtime-mini is strongly recommended as the default. The quality gap vs. gpt-realtime-1.5 is small for transcription-only use (no audio output), but the cost difference is ~5×. --- ## 7. Implementation Effort | Phase | Effort | Risk | |---|---|---| | Phase 0: Docker + deploy setup | 0.5 day | Low | | Phase 1: Quick mode merge | 2 days | Low — Hey Chill code is clean and well-isolated | | Phase 2: Post-processing UX + inspire endpoint | 2 days | Low — follows existing Brainwave patterns exactly | | Phase 3: PWA + wake word + polish | 1 day | Low — mostly copy files, light CSS work | | Phase 4: DNS cutover | 0.5 day | Low with parallel period | | **Total** | **~6 days** | **Low overall** | **Key complexity areas to watch:** 1. **CORS**: When backend is on a separate domain from the static frontend (Vercel → Railway), all `/api/*` endpoints need CORS configured for the frontend origin. 2. **WebSocket in Quick mode**: Quick mode should NOT connect a WebSocket — only Brainstorm mode should. Ensure Quick mode path stays entirely browser-side. 3. **Backend URL configuration**: Currently Brainwave assumes same-origin (`/api/v1/ws`). Need a `BACKEND_URL` env var or build-time config that the frontend uses. A single line in `main.js` handles this. 4. **Service worker caching**: The SW must not cache WebSocket connections or API calls. Cache only static assets. The existing Hey Chill `sw.js` already does this correctly. --- ## 8. Summary Recommendation ``` Short answer: Fork Brainwave, add Hey Chill's Quick mode + PWA shell, deploy backend to self-hosted Docker (192.168.101.151) behind Cloudflare Tunnel, serve static assets via Vercel (free). ~6 days of work. ~$1–2/month in API costs for personal use. ``` The fork-and-merge approach is correct — Brainwave has the hard parts (Realtime API, audio resampling, streaming LLM, IndexedDB replay) and Hey Chill has the right UX shell (two modes, message history, wake word, PWA). The two are architecturally compatible: Brainwave's backend stays unchanged; only the frontend gains new capabilities. The `/api/v1/inspire` endpoint is a 30-line addition following the exact pattern of the existing `/readability` and `/correctness` endpoints. --- ## Status DONE ## What Changed - No files changed — architecture review only, output to stdout as requested ## Key Decisions - Recommended self-hosted Docker on 192.168.101.151 for Phase 1 (zero cost, already available infrastructure) with Railway/Fly.io as upgrade path for public traffic - Recommended hybrid deployment: static assets on Vercel (free), API backend on persistent container host (WebSocket requirement rules out Vercel serverless) - Recommended `gpt-realtime-mini` as default model — ~5× cheaper than gpt-realtime-1.5 with negligible quality difference for transcription-only mode - Proposed `/api/v1/inspire` as new endpoint (30-line addition) rather than overloading existing `/correctness` endpoint, to keep prompt separation clean - Recommended phased migration (4 phases) rather than big-bang rewrite to avoid breaking the existing working PWA ## PR / Branch - None — architecture review only

Fly.io is better if Docker is already in the workflow. Neither supports static hosting well \u2014 keep static assets on Vercel (or serve from FastAPI's `StaticFiles` mount, which Brainwave already does).\n\n**Hybrid deployment (recommended for production):**\n\n```\nVercel (static CDN)                     Railway / Fly.io / Self-hosted\n    \u2502                                           \u2502\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 index.html                              \u251c\u2500\u2500 FastAPI /api/v1/ws\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 app.js                                  \u251c\u2500\u2500 /api/v1/readability\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 style.css                               \u251c\u2500\u2500 /api/v1/correctness\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 sw.js                                   \u2514\u2500\u2500 /api/v1/inspire\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 manifest.json\n            \u2502 WebSocket / fetch to BACKEND_URL\n            \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25ba\n```\n\nThe frontend config just needs `BACKEND_URL` set (currently hardcoded as relative path \u2014 needs one change to support cross-origin backend).\n\n---\n\n## 5. Migration Plan (Phased)\n\n### Phase 0 \u2014 Setup (Day 1)\n- Fork Brainwave \u2192 new repo (e.g., `hey-chill-v2` or rename)\n- Add `Dockerfile` + `docker-compose.yml`\n- Deploy to self-hosted Docker host (192.168.101.151)\n- Verify existing Brainwave functionality works at new URL\n- Add `BACKEND_URL` config to frontend (replace relative `/api` with configurable base URL)\n\n**Deliverable:** Brainwave running on Docker, accessible at `https://chill.yourdomain.com/api`\n\n### Phase 1 \u2014 Add Quick Mode (2\u20133 days)\n- Merge Hey Chill's `app.js` Quick mode section into `main.js`\n  - `startListening('quick')` with Web Speech API\n  - 3.5 s silence auto-stop\n  - Webhook POST\n  - Message history panel\n  - Settings modal (webhook URL, language, summarize URL)\n- Update `realtime.html` with two-button layout\n- Update `style.css` with Hey Chill's mode-button design\n- **No backend changes needed for this phase**\n\n**Deliverable:** Both Quick mode (Web Speech) and Brainstorm mode (Realtime API) work. Quick mode needs zero backend.\n\n### Phase 2 \u2014 Post-processing UX (2\u20133 days)\n- Update brainstorm stop flow:\n  - Show raw transcript in textarea (as now)\n  - Show two action buttons: \"Readability\" and \"Inspire / Correct\"\n  - Remove the old single Correctness button\n- Add `/api/v1/inspire` endpoint + prompt to backend\n- Wire up streaming response into enhanced textarea\n- Add optional webhook send after enhancement\n- Add \"Inspire\" tab to existing enhanced textarea area\n\n**Deliverable:** Full post-processing pipeline working as Kim specified.\n\n### Phase 3 \u2014 PWA + Polish (1\u20132 days)\n- Copy `manifest.json`, `sw.js`, `icons/` from Hey Chill\n- Add wake word (\"Hey Chill\" \u2192 triggers brainstorm recording)\n- Dark/light theme toggle (already in Brainwave CSS)\n- Mobile viewport polish\n- Update `sw.js` cache list for new file names\n\n**Deliverable:** Installable PWA, wake word, polished mobile UX.\n\n### Phase 4 \u2014 DNS Cutover (1 day)\n- Point `heychill.yourdomain.com` to new deployment\n- Old Hey Chill Vercel deployment remains live during parallel period\n- Communicate to Kim for sign-off before switching DNS\n\n---\n\n## 6. Cost Estimates\n\n### OpenAI Realtime API (per session)\n\nThe Realtime API charges for audio input tokens. Audio tokens: **1 second \u2248 25 tokens** (PCM16 at 24 kHz, OpenAI's encoding).\n\n| Session length | Audio tokens | gpt-realtime-mini cost | gpt-realtime-1.5 cost |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 2 min brainstorm | 3,000 | ~$0.008 | ~$0.036 |\n| 5 min brainstorm | 7,500 | ~$0.019 | ~$0.090 |\n| 10 min brainstorm | 15,000 | ~$0.038 | ~$0.180 |\n\n> Pricing basis: gpt-realtime-mini ~$2.50/1M audio input, ~$10/1M text output; gpt-realtime-1.5 ~$12/1M audio input. Text output (transcript tokens) is ~200\u2013500 tokens for a 5-min session \u2014 negligible cost.\n\n### Post-processing LLM (per session, GPT-4o)\n\nAfter brainstorm, user clicks one of two actions:\n\n| Call | Input tokens | Output tokens | GPT-4o cost |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| Readability (500-word transcript) | ~700 | ~700 | ~$0.007 |\n| Inspire/Correct (500-word transcript) | ~700 | ~500 | ~$0.006 |\n\n> GPT-4o pricing: $2.50/1M input, $10/1M output (as of early 2026 \u2014 verify at time of implementation).\n\n### Total Per-Session Cost\n\n| Scenario | Realtime (mini) | Post-processing | Total |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 2-min session + readability | $0.008 | $0.007 | **~$0.015** |\n| 5-min session + inspire | $0.019 | $0.006 | **~$0.025** |\n| 10-min session + both actions | $0.038 | $0.013 | **~$0.051** |\n\n**Monthly cost estimate** (assuming ~50 brainstorm sessions/month, 5 min average):\n- ~50 \u00d7 $0.025 = **~$1.25/month** in API costs for personal use\n- Quick mode (Web Speech API): **$0** \u2014 free, browser-native\n\n**Note:** gpt-realtime-mini is strongly recommended as the default. The quality gap vs. gpt-realtime-1.5 is small for transcription-only use (no audio output), but the cost difference is ~5\u00d7.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Implementation Effort\n\n| Phase | Effort | Risk |\n|---|---|---|\n| Phase 0: Docker + deploy setup | 0.5 day | Low |\n| Phase 1: Quick mode merge | 2 days | Low \u2014 Hey Chill code is clean and well-isolated |\n| Phase 2: Post-processing UX + inspire endpoint | 2 days | Low \u2014 follows existing Brainwave patterns exactly |\n| Phase 3: PWA + wake word + polish | 1 day | Low \u2014 mostly copy files, light CSS work |\n| Phase 4: DNS cutover | 0.5 day | Low with parallel period |\n| **Total** | **~6 days** | **Low overall** |\n\n**Key complexity areas to watch:**\n1. **CORS**: When backend is on a separate domain from the static frontend (Vercel \u2192 Railway), all `/api/*` endpoints need CORS configured for the frontend origin.\n2. **WebSocket in Quick mode**: Quick mode should NOT connect a WebSocket \u2014 only Brainstorm mode should. Ensure Quick mode path stays entirely browser-side.\n3. **Backend URL configuration**: Currently Brainwave assumes same-origin (`/api/v1/ws`). Need a `BACKEND_URL` env var or build-time config that the frontend uses. A single line in `main.js` handles this.\n4. **Service worker caching**: The SW must not cache WebSocket connections or API calls. Cache only static assets. The existing Hey Chill `sw.js` already does this correctly.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Summary Recommendation\n\n```\nShort answer: Fork Brainwave, add Hey Chill's Quick mode + PWA shell,\ndeploy backend to self-hosted Docker (192.168.101.151) behind Cloudflare Tunnel,\nserve static assets via Vercel (free). \n\n~6 days of work. ~$1\u20132/month in API costs for personal use.\n```\n\nThe fork-and-merge approach is correct \u2014 Brainwave has the hard parts (Realtime API, audio resampling, streaming LLM, IndexedDB replay) and Hey Chill has the right UX shell (two modes, message history, wake word, PWA). The two are architecturally compatible: Brainwave's backend stays unchanged; only the frontend gains new capabilities. The `/api/v1/inspire` endpoint is a 30-line addition following the exact pattern of the existing `/readability` and `/correctness` endpoints.\n\n---\n\n## Status\nDONE\n\n## What Changed\n- No files changed \u2014 architecture review only, output to stdout as requested\n\n## Key Decisions\n- Recommended self-hosted Docker on 192.168.101.151 for Phase 1 (zero cost, already available infrastructure) with Railway/Fly.io as upgrade path for public traffic\n- Recommended hybrid deployment: static assets on Vercel (free), API backend on persistent container host (WebSocket requirement rules out Vercel serverless)\n- Recommended `gpt-realtime-mini` as default model \u2014 ~5\u00d7 cheaper than gpt-realtime-1.5 with negligible quality difference for transcription-only mode\n- Proposed `/api/v1/inspire` as new endpoint (30-line addition) rather than overloading existing `/correctness` endpoint, to keep prompt separation clean\n- Recommended phased migration (4 phases) rather than big-bang rewrite to avoid breaking the existing working PWA\n\n## PR / Branch\n- None \u2014 architecture review only"
